Now I'm planning the game engine service in Go using Fiber to run on Zynq nodes. I'll organize it with command entry points, internal packages for auth, game logic, WebSocket handling, and database connections, plus a scoring module for exponential decay calculations. I'm setting up multi-stage Docker builds to generate optimized bare binaries, and pulling in Fiber and related dependencies.

For the API, I'm designing endpoints for authentication, map retrieval, game room management, and guess submission, with a WebSocket connection for real-time events like player joins, round starts, and score updates, plus a LiveKit integration for voice tokens.

The scoring formula uses exponential decay based on distance with a floor mismatch penalty, and I'm containerizing this with a multi-architecture Docker build that produces a static binary for ARM and x86 platforms.

Now I'm reconsidering the architecture—the auth service is actually integrated into the Game Engine itself, handling JWT validation and user management, while the stateless Zynq nodes validate tokens through middleware using Valkey for session and refresh token storage.

So the cleaner approach is to combine the Game Engine and Auth into a single service running on Zynq nodes using Fiber, handling both authentication endpoints and game logic with WebSocket support, while keeping the Worker Service separate as a Python FastAPI component.

For the Worker Service, I'm thinking it should handle the async tasks like tiling, moderation, and ELO calculations on the Main PC, and also expose admin REST endpoints so the admin panel can communicate directly with it for uploads and management operations.

Nginx will route API requests to the Zynq devices in a round-robin pattern, handle admin requests through the worker service, proxy WebSocket connections, and direct S3 requests to MinIO. # GSSR — Detailed Implementation Plan

## Context
GeoGuessr School Edition: self-hosted multiplayer panorama guessing game.
Stack: Go Fiber (game engine on Zynq ARM nodes), Python FastAPI+Celery (workers on Main PC), React+Vite (frontend + admin), infra via Docker Compose, CI/CD via GitHub Actions → DockerHub.
Repo is empty — full greenfield implementation.

---

## Monorepo Layout

```
gssr/
├── services/
│   ├── game/          # Go Fiber — Auth + Game Engine (Zynq nodes)
│   └── workers/       # Python FastAPI + Celery (Main PC)
├── frontend/          # React + Vite — игровой UI (Cloudflare Pages)
├── admin/             # React + Vite — Admin Panel (Cloudflare Pages)
├── infra/
│   ├── nginx/         # nginx.conf + upstream Zynq config
│   ├── compose/       # docker-compose.mainpc.yml + zynq template
│   └── cloudflare/    # cloudflared tunnel config (YAML)
├── migrations/        # SQL migrations (goose)
├── .github/
│   └── workflows/
└── docs/
```

---

## Plan 1: Game Engine Service (Go Fiber — Zynq nodes)

**Files:** `services/game/`

### Directory Structure
```
services/game/
├── cmd/server/
│   └── main.go             # entrypoint: fiber app setup, routes, graceful shutdown
├── internal/
│   ├── config/
│   │   └── config.go       # env vars via os.Getenv: VALKEY_URL, JWT_SECRET, etc.
│   ├── auth/
│   │   ├── handler.go      # POST /api/auth/register, /login, /refresh, /logout
│   │   ├── middleware.go   # JWT validation fiber middleware
│   │   └── jwt.go          # sign/verify, github.com/golang-jwt/jwt/v5
│   ├── user/
│   │   └── handler.go      # GET /api/users/me, PUT /api/users/me (avatar upload trigger)
│   ├── map/
│   │   └── handler.go      # GET /api/maps, GET /api/maps/:id (floors + panoramas list)
│   ├── room/
│   │   ├── handler.go      # POST /api/rooms, GET /api/rooms/:id, POST /api/rooms/:id/join
│   │   ├── manager.go      # in-process room registry (backed by Valkey)
│   │   └── state.go        # RoomState struct synced to Valkey JSON
│   ├── game/
│   │   ├── handler.go      # POST /api/rooms/:id/start, /guess, /next-round
│   │   └── scoring.go      # Score = Smax * exp(-(d/K)), floor mismatch → 0
│   ├── ws/
│   │   ├── hub.go          # WebSocket hub: subscribe/broadcast per room
│   │   └── handler.go      # GET /ws/rooms/:id  (gofiber/websocket)
│   ├── livekit/
│   │   └── handler.go      # POST /api/livekit/token (livekit-server-sdk-go)
│   └── db/
│       ├── postgres.go     # pgx/v5 pool, connection from POSTGRES_URL
│       └── valkey.go       # go-redis/v9 client
├── Makefile                # make build-amd64, build-arm, docker-build
├── Dockerfile              # multi-stage: golang:1.22-alpine → scratch, ARG TARGETARCH
└── go.mod
```

### Key Dependencies (go.mod)
```
github.com/gofiber/fiber/v2
github.com/gofiber/contrib/websocket  (gofiber websocket v2 wrapper)
github.com/golang-jwt/jwt/v5
github.com/redis/go-redis/v9
github.com/jackc/pgx/v5
github.com/google/uuid
github.com/livekit/server-sdk-go
```

### REST API Endpoints
| Method | Path | Auth | Description |
|--------|------|------|-------------|
| POST | /api/auth/register | — | create user, hash bcrypt |
| POST | /api/auth/login | — | return access+refresh JWT в HttpOnly cookie |
| POST | /api/auth/refresh | cookie | rotate refresh token |
| POST | /api/auth/logout | cookie | revoke refresh in Valkey |
| GET | /api/users/me | JWT | profile + ELO |
| GET | /api/maps | JWT | list all maps |
| GET | /api/maps/:id | JWT | map detail + floors + panorama count |
| POST | /api/rooms | JWT | create room (map_id, max_players, rounds) |
| GET | /api/rooms/:id | JWT | room state |
| POST | /api/rooms/:id/join | JWT | join room |
| POST | /api/rooms/:id/start | JWT (host) | start game |
| POST | /api/rooms/:id/guess | JWT | submit guess {pano_id, x, y, floor_id} |
| GET | /api/rooms/:id/results | JWT | round/game results |
| POST | /api/livekit/token | JWT | generate LK access token for room |

### WebSocket Events (`/ws/rooms/:id`)
```
server → client:
  player_joined   { user_id, username, avatar }
  player_left     { user_id }
  round_started   { round, pano_id, time_limit_sec }
  guess_broadcast { user_id, x, y, floor_id }   (after all guessed or timeout)
  round_ended     { scores: [{user_id, score, distance}], correct: {x,y,floor} }
  game_ended      { leaderboard: [{user_id, total_score, elo_delta}] }

client → server:
  ping / pong
```

### Scoring Logic (`internal/game/scoring.go`)
```go
const Smax = 5000.0
func CalculateScore(gx, gy, ax, ay float64, gFloor, aFloor int, K float64) int {
    if gFloor != aFloor { return 0 }
    d := math.Sqrt(math.Pow(gx-ax, 2) + math.Pow(gy-ay, 2))
    return int(Smax * math.Exp(-(d / K)))
}
```

### Deployment Modes
- **Docker** (preferred): `docker pull user/gssr-game:latest` → `docker run --env-file .env`
- **Bare binary**: `make build-arm` → `CGO_ENABLED=0 GOOS=linux GOARCH=arm GOARM=7 go build -o game-server` → SCP + systemd service

## Plan 2: Worker Service (Python FastAPI + Celery — Main PC)

**Files:** `services/workers/`

### Directory Structure
```
services/workers/
├── app/
│   ├── main.py              # FastAPI app, mounts routers, CORS (admin only)
│   ├── config.py            # pydantic-settings: PG URL, MinIO, RabbitMQ, etc.
│   ├── api/
│   │   ├── admin_maps.py    # POST /admin/maps, /maps/:id/floors
│   │   ├── admin_panos.py   # POST /admin/panoramas (upload → task), GET /pending, approve/reject
│   │   ├── admin_users.py   # GET /admin/users, PUT /admin/users/:id/ban
│   │   └── health.py        # GET /health
│   ├── tasks/
│   │   ├── celery_app.py    # Celery instance, broker=rabbitmq, backend=valkey
│   │   ├── tiling.py        # tile_panorama(pano_id): pyvips DeepZoom → MinIO /maps/{id}/panoramas/{pano_id}/
│   │   ├── moderation.py    # moderate_panorama(pano_id): onnxruntime NSFW model inference
│   │   └── elo.py           # recalculate_elo(match_id): consume RabbitMQ event from game engine
│   ├── db/
│   │   ├── base.py          # SQLAlchemy async engine
│   │   └── models.py        # ORM models mirroring SQL schema
│   └── storage/
│       └── minio_client.py  # boto3 S3 client wrapper
├── celery_worker.py         # entrypoint: celery -A app.tasks.celery_app worker
├── Dockerfile
├── requirements.txt
└── pyproject.toml
```

### Key Dependencies
```
fastapi uvicorn[standard]
celery[librabbitmq]
sqlalchemy[asyncio] asyncpg
pyvips                # libvips Python bindings (apt: libvips-dev)
boto3                 # MinIO S3
onnxruntime           # NSFW model inference
Pillow
pika                  # RabbitMQ consumer for ELO
pydantic-settings
```

### Admin REST API
| Method | Path | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| POST | /admin/maps | create map (name, x_min, x_max, y_min, y_max) |
| POST | /admin/maps/:id/floors | upload floor image → MinIO, create Floor record |
| POST | /admin/panoramas | upload equirectangular JPEG/PNG → trigger tile_panorama + moderate_panorama |
| GET | /admin/panoramas/pending | moderation queue (NSFW flagged or manual review) |
| POST | /admin/panoramas/:id/approve | set status=published |
| POST | /admin/panoramas/:id/reject | set status=rejected + delete tiles from MinIO |
| GET | /admin/users | paginated user list |
| PUT | /admin/users/:id/ban | set banned=true |
| GET | /admin/stats | total maps/panos/players/matches |

### Celery Task Flow
```
upload panorama
    → tile_panorama.delay(pano_id)
          libvips.Image.dzsave() → DeepZoom tiles
          upload to MinIO: /maps/{map_id}/panoramas/{pano_id}/{level}/{x}_{y}.webp
          update DB: pano.tile_status = "tiled"
    → moderate_panorama.delay(pano_id)  (parallel)
          onnxruntime NSFW model → score
          if score > threshold: pano.moderation = "flagged"
          else: pano.moderation = "clean"

match end event (RabbitMQ)
    → recalculate_elo(match_id)
          fetch match results
          Elo formula per player
          UPDATE users SET elo = ...
```

### MinIO Path Convention
```
/maps/{map_id}/floors/{floor_id}.webp
/maps/{map_id}/panoramas/{pano_id}/{zoom_level}/{col}_{row}.webp
/avatars/{user_id}.webp
```

### Key Dependencies

Note: Marzipano used as UMD via `<script>` tag or ESM import from npm.

### Game Flow (Game.tsx state machine)
```
WAITING → ROUND_ACTIVE → GUESSING → ROUND_RESULTS → (next round / GAME_OVER)

ROUND_ACTIVE:
  - PanoramaViewer shows current panorama tiles
  - GuessMap allows placing pin
  - FloorSelector for multi-floor maps
  - Timer countdown
  - VoiceChat always visible

GUESSING (after submit or timeout):
  - GuessMap shows all players' pins
  - correct location revealed

ROUND_RESULTS:
  - ScoreBoard with distances + scores
  - Transition to next round after N seconds
```

## Plan 5: Infrastructure (Main PC — Docker Compose + Nginx)

**Files:** `infra/`

### docker-compose.mainpc.yml
```yaml
services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:16-alpine
    volumes: [pgdata:/var/lib/postgresql/data]
    env: POSTGRES_DB, POSTGRES_USER, POSTGRES_PASSWORD

  valkey:
    image: valkey/valkey:7-alpine
    command: valkey-server --save 60 1

  rabbitmq:
    image: rabbitmq:3.13-management-alpine
    ports: [15672]  # management UI (internal only)

  minio:
    image: minio/minio:latest
    command: server /data --console-address ":9001"
    volumes: [minio_data:/data]
    env: MINIO_ROOT_USER, MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD

  workers:
    image: user/gssr-workers:latest
    depends_on: [postgres, valkey, rabbitmq, minio]
    env_file: .env.workers

  celery:
    image: user/gssr-workers:latest
    command: celery -A app.tasks.celery_app worker -l info -Q default
    depends_on: [rabbitmq, valkey]
    env_file: .env.workers

  livekit:
    image: livekit/livekit-server:latest
    command: --config /etc/livekit.yaml
    volumes: [./livekit.yaml:/etc/livekit.yaml]

  nginx:
    image: nginx:1.27-alpine
    volumes:
      - ./infra/nginx/nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf:ro
      - ./infra/nginx/upstream.conf:/etc/nginx/conf.d/upstream.conf:ro
    ports: [80, 443]
    depends_on: [workers, minio, livekit]

  cloudflared:
    image: cloudflare/cloudflared:latest
    command: tunnel --config /etc/cf/config.yml run
    volumes: [./infra/cloudflare:/etc/cf:ro]
```

### Nginx Configuration (`infra/nginx/nginx.conf`)
```nginx
upstream zynq_game {
    least_conn;
    server zynq1:3000;
    server zynq2:3000;
    server zynq3:3000;
    server zynq4:3000;
    server zynq5:3000;
}

# /api/* → Zynq round-robin (except /api/admin/*)
# /api/admin/* → workers:8000
# /ws/* → Zynq (upgrade: WebSocket)
# /s3/* → minio:9000 (proxy pass, strip prefix)
# /livekit/* → livekit:7880
```

### Database Migrations (`migrations/`)
Using **goose** (SQL-based, no ORM lock-in):
```
migrations/
├── 00001_create_users.sql
├── 00002_create_maps.sql
├── 00003_create_floors.sql
├── 00004_create_panoramas.sql
├── 00005_create_matches.sql
└── 00006_create_guesses.sql
```

Key schema:
```sql
-- users: id, username, password_hash, avatar_url, elo, banned, created_at
-- maps: id, name, x_min, x_max, y_min, y_max, coord_type
-- floors: id, map_id, floor_number, image_url
-- panoramas: id, floor_id, x, y, north_offset, tile_status, moderation_status
-- matches: id, room_id, map_id, started_at, ended_at
-- guesses: id, match_id, user_id, panorama_id, guess_x, guess_y, guess_floor_id, score
```

### Zynq Deployment (`infra/compose/docker-compose.zynq.yml`)
```yaml
services:
  game:
    image: user/gssr-game:latest
    platform: linux/arm/v7
    env_file: .env.zynq
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports: [3000:3000]
```

Bare binary alternative: `infra/zynq/deploy.sh` — SCP binary + restart systemd unit.

---

## Plan 6: CI/CD (GitHub Actions + DockerHub)

**Files:** `.github/workflows/`

### Workflow 1: `build-game.yml`
Trigger: push to `main` or tag `game/v*`
```yaml
- name: Set up QEMU        # for arm/v7 emulation
- name: Set up buildx
- name: Login to DockerHub
- name: Build & push
  uses: docker/build-push-action
  with:
    context: services/game
    platforms: linux/amd64,linux/arm/v7
    tags: user/gssr-game:latest,user/gssr-game:${{ github.sha }}
    cache-from: type=gha
    cache-to: type=gha,mode=max
```

### Workflow 2: `build-workers.yml`
Trigger: push to `main` or tag `workers/v*`
Same structure, single platform `linux/amd64`.

### Workflow 3: `deploy-frontend.yml`
Trigger: push to `main`, path `frontend/**`
```yaml
- npm ci && npm run build
- uses: cloudflare/wrangler-action
  with:
    command: pages deploy dist --project-name=gssr-frontend
```

### Workflow 4: `deploy-admin.yml`
Same as frontend, path `admin/**`, project-name=`gssr-admin`.

### Workflow 5: `deploy-mainpc.yml`
Trigger: after `build-game.yml` and `build-workers.yml` complete (workflow_run)
```yaml
- name: Deploy via SSH
  uses: appleboy/ssh-action
  with:
    host: ${{ secrets.MAINPC_HOST }}
    key: ${{ secrets.MAINPC_SSH_KEY }}
    script: |
      cd /opt/gssr
      docker-compose -f docker-compose.mainpc.yml pull
      docker-compose -f docker-compose.mainpc.yml up -d --no-build
      # Run migrations
      docker run --rm --network gssr_default \
        -e DATABASE_URL=$DATABASE_URL \
        ghcr.io/pressly/goose:latest postgres "$DATABASE_URL" up
```

### Workflow 6: `deploy-zynq.yml`
Trigger: after `build-game.yml` (workflow_run)
```yaml
strategy:
  matrix:
    zynq: [zynq1, zynq2, zynq3, zynq4, zynq5]
- name: Docker pull on Zynq (if Docker available)
  uses: appleboy/ssh-action (per host)
  script: docker pull user/gssr-game:latest && docker-compose up -d --no-build
- name: Bare binary fallback
  # if docker fails: scp game-server-arm binary, systemctl restart gssr-game
```

### Required GitHub Secrets
```
DOCKERHUB_USERNAME / DOCKERHUB_TOKEN
CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN / CLOUDFLARE_ACCOUNT_ID
MAINPC_SSH_HOST / MAINPC_SSH_KEY
ZYNQ1_HOST … ZYNQ5_HOST
ZYNQ_SSH_KEY  (shared key for all Zynq nodes)
DATABASE_URL   (for migration step)
```

---

## Implementation Order

1. **`migrations/`** — схема БД (goose SQL)
2. **`infra/`** — docker-compose + nginx config (локальный стенд на Main PC)
3. **`services/game`** — Go Fiber: auth → rooms → WS → scoring
4. **`services/workers`** — FastAPI + tiling + NSFW + ELO worker
5. **`frontend/`** — React game UI (без LiveKit на старте, добавить позже)
6. **`admin/`** — React admin panel
7. **`.github/workflows/`** — CI/CD после того, как всё работает локально

---

## Verification / Testing Checklist

- `docker-compose up -d` на Main PC → все сервисы healthy
- `goose up` → миграции применились, schema корректна
- Game Engine: `curl -X POST /api/auth/register` → JWT cookie
- Game Engine: создать room, join 2 игрока, WebSocket events приходят
- Workers: загрузить 8K панораму → тайлы появились в MinIO
- Workers: NSFW сцена → статус `flagged`, чистое фото → `clean`
- Frontend: Marzipano рендерит тайлы, Leaflet принимает клик → очки считаются
- CI: push в main → DockerHub образ пересобирается, Main PC деплоится автоматически
- Zynq: docker pull нового образа ИЛИ SCP бинаря → сервис рестартует без даунтайма
Claude’s Plan
GSSR — Detailed Implementation Plan
Context
GeoGuessr School Edition: self-hosted multiplayer panorama guessing game.
Stack: Go Fiber (game engine on Zynq ARM nodes), Python FastAPI+Celery (workers on Main PC), React+Vite (frontend + admin), infra via Docker Compose, CI/CD via GitHub Actions → DockerHub.
Repo is empty — full greenfield implementation.

Monorepo Layout

gssr/
├── services/
│   ├── game/          # Go Fiber — Auth + Game Engine (Zynq nodes)
│   └── workers/       # Python FastAPI + Celery (Main PC)
├── frontend/          # React + Vite — игровой UI (Cloudflare Pages)
├── admin/             # React + Vite — Admin Panel (Cloudflare Pages)
├── infra/
│   ├── nginx/         # nginx.conf + upstream Zynq config
│   ├── compose/       # docker-compose.mainpc.yml + zynq template
│   └── cloudflare/    # cloudflared tunnel config (YAML)
├── migrations/        # SQL migrations (goose)
├── .github/
│   └── workflows/
└── docs/
Plan 1: Game Engine Service (Go Fiber — Zynq nodes)
Files: services/game/

Directory Structure

services/game/
├── cmd/server/
│   └── main.go             # entrypoint: fiber app setup, routes, graceful shutdown
├── internal/
│   ├── config/
│   │   └── config.go       # env vars via os.Getenv: VALKEY_URL, JWT_SECRET, etc.
│   ├── auth/
│   │   ├── handler.go      # POST /api/auth/register, /login, /refresh, /logout
│   │   ├── middleware.go   # JWT validation fiber middleware
│   │   └── jwt.go          # sign/verify, github.com/golang-jwt/jwt/v5
│   ├── user/
│   │   └── handler.go      # GET /api/users/me, PUT /api/users/me (avatar upload trigger)
│   ├── map/
│   │   └── handler.go      # GET /api/maps, GET /api/maps/:id (floors + panoramas list)
│   ├── room/
│   │   ├── handler.go      # POST /api/rooms, GET /api/rooms/:id, POST /api/rooms/:id/join
│   │   ├── manager.go      # in-process room registry (backed by Valkey)
│   │   └── state.go        # RoomState struct synced to Valkey JSON
│   ├── game/
│   │   ├── handler.go      # POST /api/rooms/:id/start, /guess, /next-round
│   │   └── scoring.go      # Score = Smax * exp(-(d/K)), floor mismatch → 0
│   ├── ws/
│   │   ├── hub.go          # WebSocket hub: subscribe/broadcast per room
│   │   └── handler.go      # GET /ws/rooms/:id  (gofiber/websocket)
│   ├── livekit/
│   │   └── handler.go      # POST /api/livekit/token (livekit-server-sdk-go)
│   └── db/
│       ├── postgres.go     # pgx/v5 pool, connection from POSTGRES_URL
│       └── valkey.go       # go-redis/v9 client
├── Makefile                # make build-amd64, build-arm, docker-build
├── Dockerfile              # multi-stage: golang:1.22-alpine → scratch, ARG TARGETARCH
└── go.mod
Key Dependencies (go.mod)

github.com/gofiber/fiber/v2
github.com/gofiber/contrib/websocket  (gofiber websocket v2 wrapper)
github.com/golang-jwt/jwt/v5
github.com/redis/go-redis/v9
github.com/jackc/pgx/v5
github.com/google/uuid
github.com/livekit/server-sdk-go
REST API Endpoints
Method	Path	Auth	Description
POST	/api/auth/register	—	create user, hash bcrypt
POST	/api/auth/login	—	return access+refresh JWT в HttpOnly cookie
POST	/api/auth/refresh	cookie	rotate refresh token
POST	/api/auth/logout	cookie	revoke refresh in Valkey
GET	/api/users/me	JWT	profile + ELO
GET	/api/maps	JWT	list all maps
GET	/api/maps/:id	JWT	map detail + floors + panorama count
POST	/api/rooms	JWT	create room (map_id, max_players, rounds)
GET	/api/rooms/:id	JWT	room state
POST	/api/rooms/:id/join	JWT	join room
POST	/api/rooms/:id/start	JWT (host)	start game
POST	/api/rooms/:id/guess	JWT	submit guess {pano_id, x, y, floor_id}
GET	/api/rooms/:id/results	JWT	round/game results
POST	/api/livekit/token	JWT	generate LK access token for room
WebSocket Events (/ws/rooms/:id)

server → client:
  player_joined   { user_id, username, avatar }
  player_left     { user_id }
  round_started   { round, pano_id, time_limit_sec }
  guess_broadcast { user_id, x, y, floor_id }   (after all guessed or timeout)
  round_ended     { scores: [{user_id, score, distance}], correct: {x,y,floor} }
  game_ended      { leaderboard: [{user_id, total_score, elo_delta}] }

client → server:
  ping / pong
Scoring Logic (internal/game/scoring.go)

const Smax = 5000.0
func CalculateScore(gx, gy, ax, ay float64, gFloor, aFloor int, K float64) int {
    if gFloor != aFloor { return 0 }
    d := math.Sqrt(math.Pow(gx-ax, 2) + math.Pow(gy-ay, 2))
    return int(Smax * math.Exp(-(d / K)))
}
Deployment Modes
Docker (preferred): docker pull user/gssr-game:latest → docker run --env-file .env
Bare binary: make build-arm → CGO_ENABLED=0 GOOS=linux GOARCH=arm GOARM=7 go build -o game-server → SCP + systemd service
Plan 2: Worker Service (Python FastAPI + Celery — Main PC)
Files: services/workers/

Directory Structure

services/workers/
├── app/
│   ├── main.py              # FastAPI app, mounts routers, CORS (admin only)
│   ├── config.py            # pydantic-settings: PG URL, MinIO, RabbitMQ, etc.
│   ├── api/
│   │   ├── admin_maps.py    # POST /admin/maps, /maps/:id/floors
│   │   ├── admin_panos.py   # POST /admin/panoramas (upload → task), GET /pending, approve/reject
│   │   ├── admin_users.py   # GET /admin/users, PUT /admin/users/:id/ban
│   │   └── health.py        # GET /health
│   ├── tasks/
│   │   ├── celery_app.py    # Celery instance, broker=rabbitmq, backend=valkey
│   │   ├── tiling.py        # tile_panorama(pano_id): pyvips DeepZoom → MinIO /maps/{id}/panoramas/{pano_id}/
│   │   ├── moderation.py    # moderate_panorama(pano_id): onnxruntime NSFW model inference
│   │   └── elo.py           # recalculate_elo(match_id): consume RabbitMQ event from game engine
│   ├── db/
│   │   ├── base.py          # SQLAlchemy async engine
│   │   └── models.py        # ORM models mirroring SQL schema
│   └── storage/
│       └── minio_client.py  # boto3 S3 client wrapper
├── celery_worker.py         # entrypoint: celery -A app.tasks.celery_app worker
├── Dockerfile
├── requirements.txt
└── pyproject.toml
Key Dependencies

fastapi uvicorn[standard]
celery[librabbitmq]
sqlalchemy[asyncio] asyncpg
pyvips                # libvips Python bindings (apt: libvips-dev)
boto3                 # MinIO S3
onnxruntime           # NSFW model inference
Pillow
pika                  # RabbitMQ consumer for ELO
pydantic-settings
Admin REST API
Method	Path	Description
POST	/admin/maps	create map (name, x_min, x_max, y_min, y_max)
POST	/admin/maps/:id/floors	upload floor image → MinIO, create Floor record
POST	/admin/panoramas	upload equirectangular JPEG/PNG → trigger tile_panorama + moderate_panorama
GET	/admin/panoramas/pending	moderation queue (NSFW flagged or manual review)
POST	/admin/panoramas/:id/approve	set status=published
POST	/admin/panoramas/:id/reject	set status=rejected + delete tiles from MinIO
GET	/admin/users	paginated user list
PUT	/admin/users/:id/ban	set banned=true
GET	/admin/stats	total maps/panos/players/matches
Celery Task Flow

upload panorama
    → tile_panorama.delay(pano_id)
          libvips.Image.dzsave() → DeepZoom tiles
          upload to MinIO: /maps/{map_id}/panoramas/{pano_id}/{level}/{x}_{y}.webp
          update DB: pano.tile_status = "tiled"
    → moderate_panorama.delay(pano_id)  (parallel)
          onnxruntime NSFW model → score
          if score > threshold: pano.moderation = "flagged"
          else: pano.moderation = "clean"

match end event (RabbitMQ)
    → recalculate_elo(match_id)
          fetch match results
          Elo formula per player
          UPDATE users SET elo = ...
MinIO Path Convention

/maps/{map_id}/floors/{floor_id}.webp
/maps/{map_id}/panoramas/{pano_id}/{zoom_level}/{col}_{row}.webp
/avatars/{user_id}.webp

│   │   └── useAuth.ts               # login/logout/refresh, cookie-based
│   ├── api/
│   │   └── client.ts                # axios instance, baseURL from VITE_API_URL, withCredentials
│   ├── store/
│   │   └── gameStore.ts             # zustand: roomState, players, currentRound, myGuess
│   └── utils/

├── public/
│   └── marzipano/                   # Marzipano JS library files

├── tailwind.config.ts
└── package.json
Key Dependencies

{
  "react": "^18",

}
Note: Marzipano used as UMD via <script> tag or ESM import from npm.

Game Flow (Game.tsx state machine)

WAITING → ROUND_ACTIVE → GUESSING → ROUND_RESULTS → (next round / GAME_OVER)

ROUND_ACTIVE:
  - PanoramaViewer shows current panorama tiles
  - GuessMap allows placing pin
  - FloorSelector for multi-floor maps
  - Timer countdown
  - VoiceChat always visible

GUESSING (after submit or timeout):
  - GuessMap shows all players' pins
  - correct location revealed

ROUND_RESULTS:
  - ScoreBoard with distances + scores
  - Transition to next round after N seconds

Plan 5: Infrastructure (Main PC — Docker Compose + Nginx)
Files: infra/

docker-compose.mainpc.yml

services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:16-alpine
    volumes: [pgdata:/var/lib/postgresql/data]
    env: POSTGRES_DB, POSTGRES_USER, POSTGRES_PASSWORD

  valkey:
    image: valkey/valkey:7-alpine
    command: valkey-server --save 60 1

  rabbitmq:
    image: rabbitmq:3.13-management-alpine
    ports: [15672]  # management UI (internal only)

  minio:
    image: minio/minio:latest
    command: server /data --console-address ":9001"
    volumes: [minio_data:/data]
    env: MINIO_ROOT_USER, MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD

  workers:
    image: user/gssr-workers:latest
    depends_on: [postgres, valkey, rabbitmq, minio]
    env_file: .env.workers

  celery:
    image: user/gssr-workers:latest
    command: celery -A app.tasks.celery_app worker -l info -Q default
    depends_on: [rabbitmq, valkey]
    env_file: .env.workers

  livekit:
    image: livekit/livekit-server:latest
    command: --config /etc/livekit.yaml
    volumes: [./livekit.yaml:/etc/livekit.yaml]

  nginx:
    image: nginx:1.27-alpine
    volumes:
      - ./infra/nginx/nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf:ro
      - ./infra/nginx/upstream.conf:/etc/nginx/conf.d/upstream.conf:ro
    ports: [80, 443]
    depends_on: [workers, minio, livekit]

  cloudflared:
    image: cloudflare/cloudflared:latest
    command: tunnel --config /etc/cf/config.yml run
    volumes: [./infra/cloudflare:/etc/cf:ro]
Nginx Configuration (infra/nginx/nginx.conf)

upstream zynq_game {
    least_conn;
    server zynq1:3000;
    server zynq2:3000;
    server zynq3:3000;
    server zynq4:3000;
    server zynq5:3000;
}

# /api/* → Zynq round-robin (except /api/admin/*)
# /api/admin/* → workers:8000
# /ws/* → Zynq (upgrade: WebSocket)
# /s3/* → minio:9000 (proxy pass, strip prefix)
# /livekit/* → livekit:7880
Database Migrations (migrations/)
Using goose (SQL-based, no ORM lock-in):


migrations/
├── 00001_create_users.sql
├── 00002_create_maps.sql
├── 00003_create_floors.sql
├── 00004_create_panoramas.sql
├── 00005_create_matches.sql
└── 00006_create_guesses.sql
Key schema:


-- users: id, username, password_hash, avatar_url, elo, banned, created_at
-- maps: id, name, x_min, x_max, y_min, y_max, coord_type
-- floors: id, map_id, floor_number, image_url
-- panoramas: id, floor_id, x, y, north_offset, tile_status, moderation_status
-- matches: id, room_id, map_id, started_at, ended_at
-- guesses: id, match_id, user_id, panorama_id, guess_x, guess_y, guess_floor_id, score

    platform: linux/arm/v7
    env_file: .env.zynq
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports: [3000:3000]

k3s for Zynq:

Zynq boards are ARM v7 with OpenWrt/Linux, and while k3s technically supports ARM, the real constraint is whether OpenWrt has the kernel features k3s needs like cgroups v2. The more practical approach would be running k3s server on the main PC with agents on Zynq if the kernel supports it, though this might be pushing the limits of what those boards can handle.

If the Zynq nodes run proper Linux instead of OpenWrt, k3s becomes a viable option worth including in the deployment plan.

# GSSR — Detailed Implementation Plan

## Context

GeoGuessr School Edition: self-hosted multiplayer panorama guessing game.
Stack: Go Fiber (game engine on Zynq ARM nodes), Python FastAPI+Celery (workers on Main PC), React+Vite (frontend + admin), infra via Docker Compose, CI/CD via GitHub Actions → DockerHub.
Repo is empty — full greenfield implementation.

---

## Monorepo Layout

```text
gssr/
├── services/
│   ├── game/          # Go Fiber — Auth + Game Engine (Zynq nodes)
│   └── workers/       # Python FastAPI + Celery (Main PC)
├── frontend/          # React + Vite — игровой UI (Cloudflare Pages)
├── admin/             # React + Vite — Admin Panel (Cloudflare Pages)
├── infra/
│   ├── nginx/         # nginx.conf + upstream Zynq/k3s config
│   ├── compose/       # docker-compose.mainpc.yml + zynq template
│   ├── k8s/           # k3s manifests (Zynq cluster option)
│   ├── monitoring/    # Prometheus + Grafana + Loki stack
│   └── cloudflare/    # cloudflared tunnel config + Cloudflare Access rules
├── migrations/        # SQL migrations (goose)
├── .github/
│   └── workflows/
└── docs/
```

---

## Plan 1: Game Engine Service (Go Fiber — Zynq nodes)

**Files:** `services/game/`

### Game Service Structure

```text
services/game/
├── cmd/server/
│   └── main.go             # entrypoint: fiber app setup, routes, graceful shutdown
├── internal/
│   ├── config/
│   │   └── config.go       # env vars via os.Getenv: VALKEY_URL, JWT_SECRET, etc.
│   ├── auth/
│   │   ├── handler.go      # POST /api/auth/register, /login, /refresh, /logout
│   │   ├── middleware.go   # JWT validation fiber middleware
│   │   └── jwt.go          # sign/verify, github.com/golang-jwt/jwt/v5
│   ├── user/
│   │   └── handler.go      # GET /api/users/me, PUT /api/users/me (avatar upload trigger)
│   ├── map/
│   │   └── handler.go      # GET /api/maps, GET /api/maps/:id (floors + panoramas list)
│   ├── room/
│   │   ├── handler.go      # POST /api/rooms, GET /api/rooms/:id, POST /api/rooms/:id/join
│   │   ├── manager.go      # in-process room registry (backed by Valkey)
│   │   └── state.go        # RoomState struct synced to Valkey JSON
│   ├── game/
│   │   ├── handler.go      # POST /api/rooms/:id/start, /guess, /next-round
│   │   └── scoring.go      # Score = Smax * exp(-(d/K)), floor mismatch → 0
│   ├── ws/
│   │   ├── hub.go          # WebSocket hub: subscribe/broadcast per room
│   │   └── handler.go      # GET /ws/rooms/:id  (gofiber/websocket)
│   ├── livekit/
│   │   └── handler.go      # POST /api/livekit/token (livekit-server-sdk-go)
│   └── db/
│       ├── postgres.go     # pgx/v5 pool, connection from POSTGRES_URL
│       └── valkey.go       # go-redis/v9 client
├── Makefile                # make build-amd64, build-arm, docker-build
├── Dockerfile              # multi-stage: golang:1.22-alpine → scratch, ARG TARGETARCH
└── go.mod
```

### Go Dependencies

```text
github.com/gofiber/fiber/v2
github.com/gofiber/contrib/websocket
github.com/golang-jwt/jwt/v5
github.com/redis/go-redis/v9
github.com/jackc/pgx/v5
github.com/google/uuid
github.com/livekit/server-sdk-go
github.com/ansrivas/fiberprometheus/v2
```

### REST API Endpoints

| Method | Path | Auth | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| POST | /api/auth/register | — | create user, hash bcrypt |
| POST | /api/auth/login | — | return access+refresh JWT в HttpOnly cookie |
| POST | /api/auth/refresh | cookie | rotate refresh token |
| POST | /api/auth/logout | cookie | revoke refresh in Valkey |
| GET | /api/users/me | JWT | profile + ELO |
| GET | /api/maps | JWT | list all maps |
| GET | /api/maps/:id | JWT | map detail + floors + panorama count |
| POST | /api/rooms | JWT | create room (map_id, max_players, rounds) |
| GET | /api/rooms/:id | JWT | room state |
| POST | /api/rooms/:id/join | JWT | join room |
| POST | /api/rooms/:id/start | JWT (host) | start game |
| POST | /api/rooms/:id/guess | JWT | submit guess {pano_id, x, y, floor_id} |
| GET | /api/rooms/:id/results | JWT | round/game results |
| POST | /api/livekit/token | JWT | generate LK access token for room |

### WebSocket Events (`/ws/rooms/:id`)

```text
server → client:
  player_joined   { user_id, username, avatar }
  player_left     { user_id }
  round_started   { round, pano_id, time_limit_sec }
  guess_broadcast { user_id, x, y, floor_id }   (after all guessed or timeout)
  round_ended     { scores: [{user_id, score, distance}], correct: {x,y,floor} }
  game_ended      { leaderboard: [{user_id, total_score, elo_delta}] }

client → server:
  ping / pong
```

### Scoring Logic (`internal/game/scoring.go`)

```go
const Smax = 5000.0
func CalculateScore(gx, gy, ax, ay float64, gFloor, aFloor int, K float64) int {
    if gFloor != aFloor { return 0 }
    d := math.Sqrt(math.Pow(gx-ax, 2) + math.Pow(gy-ay, 2))
    return int(Smax * math.Exp(-(d / K)))
}
```

### Game Service Tests

```text
internal/
  auth/handler_test.go      # httptest: register, login, token rotation
  game/scoring_test.go      # table-driven unit tests for CalculateScore
  room/manager_test.go      # room state sync to Valkey (testcontainers-go Redis)
  ws/hub_test.go            # goroutine hub: broadcast, disconnect
integration/
  auth_integration_test.go  # full flow with real PG (testcontainers-go Postgres)
  game_integration_test.go  # create room → join → guess → score
```

Key tools: `testcontainers-go`, `net/http/httptest`, `github.com/stretchr/testify`

Makefile targets: `make test` (go test ./... -race), `make test-coverage` (threshold 80%)

### Game Service Deployment

- **Docker** (preferred): `docker pull user/gssr-game:latest` → `docker run --env-file .env`
- **Bare binary**: `make build-arm` → `CGO_ENABLED=0 GOOS=linux GOARCH=arm GOARM=7 go build` → SCP + systemd
- **k3s** (see Plan 9)

## Plan 2: Worker Service (Python FastAPI + Celery — Main PC)

**Files:** `services/workers/`

### Worker Service Structure

```text
services/workers/
├── app/
│   ├── main.py              # FastAPI app, mounts routers, CORS (admin only)
│   ├── config.py            # pydantic-settings: PG URL, MinIO, RabbitMQ, etc.
│   ├── api/
│   │   ├── admin_maps.py    # POST /admin/maps, /maps/:id/floors
│   │   ├── admin_panos.py   # POST /admin/panoramas, GET /pending, approve/reject
│   │   ├── admin_users.py   # GET /admin/users, PUT /admin/users/:id/ban
│   │   └── health.py        # GET /health, GET /metrics
│   ├── tasks/
│   │   ├── celery_app.py    # Celery instance, broker=rabbitmq, backend=valkey
│   │   ├── tiling.py        # tile_panorama(pano_id): pyvips DeepZoom → MinIO
│   │   ├── moderation.py    # moderate_panorama(pano_id): onnxruntime NSFW inference
│   │   └── elo.py           # recalculate_elo(match_id): consume RabbitMQ event
│   ├── db/
│   │   ├── base.py          # SQLAlchemy async engine
│   │   └── models.py        # ORM models mirroring SQL schema
│   └── storage/
│       └── minio_client.py  # boto3 S3 client wrapper
├── celery_worker.py         # entrypoint: celery -A app.tasks.celery_app worker
├── Dockerfile
├── requirements.txt
└── pyproject.toml
```

### Python Dependencies

```text
fastapi uvicorn[standard]
celery[librabbitmq]
sqlalchemy[asyncio] asyncpg
pyvips                # libvips Python bindings (apt: libvips-dev)
boto3                 # MinIO S3
onnxruntime           # NSFW model inference
Pillow
pika                  # RabbitMQ consumer for ELO
pydantic-settings
prometheus-fastapi-instrumentator
```

### Admin REST API

| Method | Path | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| POST | /admin/maps | create map (name, x_min, x_max, y_min, y_max) |
| POST | /admin/maps/:id/floors | upload floor image → MinIO, create Floor record |
| POST | /admin/panoramas | upload equirectangular JPEG/PNG → trigger tiling + moderation tasks |
| GET | /admin/panoramas/pending | moderation queue (NSFW flagged or manual review) |
| POST | /admin/panoramas/:id/approve | set status=published |
| POST | /admin/panoramas/:id/reject | set status=rejected + delete tiles from MinIO |
| GET | /admin/users | paginated user list |
| PUT | /admin/users/:id/ban | set banned=true |
| GET | /admin/stats | total maps/panos/players/matches |

### Celery Task Flow

```text
upload panorama
    → tile_panorama.delay(pano_id)
          libvips.Image.dzsave() → DeepZoom tiles
          upload to MinIO: /maps/{map_id}/panoramas/{pano_id}/{level}/{x}_{y}.webp
          update DB: pano.tile_status = "tiled"
    → moderate_panorama.delay(pano_id)  [parallel]
          onnxruntime NSFW model → score
          if score > threshold: pano.moderation = "flagged"
          else: pano.moderation = "clean"

match end event (RabbitMQ)
    → recalculate_elo(match_id)
          fetch match results, Elo formula per player
          UPDATE users SET elo = ...
```

### MinIO Path Convention

```text
/maps/{map_id}/floors/{floor_id}.webp
/maps/{map_id}/panoramas/{pano_id}/{zoom_level}/{col}_{row}.webp
/avatars/{user_id}.webp
```

### Worker Service Tests

```text
tests/
  test_api_maps.py         # pytest + httpx AsyncClient: create map, upload floor
  test_api_panos.py        # upload panorama → check task queued
  test_tasks_tiling.py     # mock pyvips + minio: tile_panorama task completes
  test_tasks_moderation.py # mock onnxruntime: score above/below threshold
  test_elo.py              # ELO formula unit tests with known inputs
conftest.py                # pytest fixtures: async engine, test DB (testcontainers), minio mock
```

Key tools: `pytest`, `pytest-asyncio`, `httpx`, `factory_boy`, `testcontainers[postgres]`, `moto` (S3 mock)

### Frontend Dependencies

```json
{
  "react": "^18",
```

Note: Marzipano used as UMD via `<script>` tag or ESM import from npm.

### Game Flow (Game.tsx state machine)

```text
WAITING → ROUND_ACTIVE → GUESSING → ROUND_RESULTS → (next round / GAME_OVER)

ROUND_ACTIVE:
  - PanoramaViewer shows current panorama tiles
  - GuessMap allows placing pin
  - FloorSelector for multi-floor maps
  - Timer countdown
  - VoiceChat always visible

GUESSING (after submit or timeout):
  - GuessMap shows all players' pins
  - correct location revealed

ROUND_RESULTS:
  - ScoreBoard with distances + scores
  - Transition to next round after N seconds
```

### Frontend Tests

```text
src/__tests__/
  scoring.test.ts            # pure CalculateScore util (identical formula in TS)
  useGameState.test.ts       # Vitest: zustand store transitions
  GuessMap.test.tsx          # React Testing Library: click places pin
  PanoramaViewer.test.tsx    # mock Marzipano, verify tile URL constructed correctly
  ScoreBoard.test.tsx        # renders correct scores and distances
  nsfwCheck.test.ts          # mock nsfwjs, verify above/below threshold behavior
e2e/
  auth.spec.ts               # Playwright: register → login → profile page
  game.spec.ts               # create room → start game → submit guess → see score
  admin.spec.ts              # upload panorama → appears in moderation queue
```

Key tools: `vitest`, `@testing-library/react`, `msw` (mock API), `playwright`

## Plan 4: Admin Panel (React + Vite — Cloudflare Pages)

**Files:** `admin/`

### Admin Panel Structure

```text
admin/
├── src/
│   ├── pages/
│   │   ├── Dashboard.tsx    # stats overview
│   │   ├── Maps.tsx         # CRUD maps, floors
│   │   ├── PanoramaUpload.tsx   # drag-drop upload, progress bar (multipart)

│   │   │   └── FloorPlanEditor.tsx   # Leaflet L.CRS.Simple, draw map boundaries

```

## Plan 5: Infrastructure (Main PC — Docker Compose + Nginx)

**Files:** `infra/`

### docker-compose.mainpc.yml

```yaml
services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:16-alpine
    volumes: [pgdata:/var/lib/postgresql/data]
    env: POSTGRES_DB, POSTGRES_USER, POSTGRES_PASSWORD

  valkey:
    image: valkey/valkey:7-alpine
    command: valkey-server --save 60 1

  rabbitmq:
    image: rabbitmq:3.13-management-alpine

  minio:
    image: minio/minio:latest
    command: server /data --console-address ":9001"
    volumes: [minio_data:/data]
    env: MINIO_ROOT_USER, MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD

  workers:
    image: user/gssr-workers:latest
    depends_on: [postgres, valkey, rabbitmq, minio]
    env_file: .env.workers

  celery:
    image: user/gssr-workers:latest
    command: celery -A app.tasks.celery_app worker -l info -Q default
    depends_on: [rabbitmq, valkey]
    env_file: .env.workers

  livekit:
    image: livekit/livekit-server:latest
    command: --config /etc/livekit.yaml
    volumes: [./livekit.yaml:/etc/livekit.yaml]

  nginx:
    image: nginx:1.27-alpine
    volumes:
      - ./infra/nginx/nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf:ro
    ports: [80, 443]

  cloudflared:
    image: cloudflare/cloudflared:latest
    command: tunnel --config /etc/cf/config.yml run
    volumes: [./infra/cloudflare:/etc/cf:ro]
```

### Nginx Routing (`infra/nginx/nginx.conf`)

```nginx
upstream zynq_game {
    least_conn;
    server zynq1:3000;
    server zynq2:3000;
    server zynq3:3000;
    server zynq4:3000;
    server zynq5:3000;
}

# /api/* → Zynq round-robin (except /api/admin/*)
# /api/admin/* → workers:8000
# /ws/* → Zynq (upgrade: WebSocket)
# /s3/* → minio:9000 (proxy pass, strip prefix)
# /livekit/* → livekit:7880
```

### Database Migrations (`migrations/`)

Using **goose** (SQL-based, no ORM lock-in):

```text
migrations/
├── 00001_create_users.sql
├── 00002_create_maps.sql
├── 00003_create_floors.sql
├── 00004_create_panoramas.sql
├── 00005_create_matches.sql
└── 00006_create_guesses.sql
```

Key schema:

```sql
-- users: id, username, password_hash, avatar_url, elo, banned, created_at
-- maps: id, name, x_min, x_max, y_min, y_max, coord_type
-- floors: id, map_id, floor_number, image_url
-- panoramas: id, floor_id, x, y, north_offset, tile_status, moderation_status
-- matches: id, room_id, map_id, started_at, ended_at
-- guesses: id, match_id, user_id, panorama_id, guess_x, guess_y, guess_floor_id, score
```

### Zynq Docker Compose (`infra/compose/docker-compose.zynq.yml`)

```yaml
services:
  game:
    image: user/gssr-game:latest
    platform: linux/arm/v7
    env_file: .env.zynq
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports: [3000:3000]
```

Bare binary alternative: `infra/zynq/deploy.sh` — SCP binary + restart systemd unit.

## Plan 6: CI/CD (GitHub Actions + DockerHub)

**Files:** `.github/workflows/`

### Workflow 1 — build-game.yml

Trigger: push to `main` or tag `game/v*`

```yaml
- name: Set up QEMU        # for arm/v7 emulation
- name: Set up buildx
- name: Login to DockerHub
- name: Build & push
  uses: docker/build-push-action
  with:
    context: services/game
    platforms: linux/amd64,linux/arm/v7
    tags: user/gssr-game:latest,user/gssr-game:${{ github.sha }}
    cache-from: type=gha
    cache-to: type=gha,mode=max
```

### Workflow 2 — build-workers.yml

Trigger: push to `main` or tag `workers/v*`

Same structure, single platform `linux/amd64`.

### Workflow 3 — deploy-frontend.yml

Trigger: push to `main`, path `frontend/**`

```yaml
- run: npm ci && npm run build
- uses: cloudflare/wrangler-action
  with:
    command: pages deploy dist --project-name=gssr-frontend
```

### Workflow 4 — deploy-admin.yml

Same as Workflow 3, path `admin/**`, project-name=`gssr-admin`.

### Workflow 5 — deploy-mainpc.yml

Trigger: after build-game + build-workers complete (`workflow_run`)

```yaml
- name: Deploy via SSH
  uses: appleboy/ssh-action
  with:
    host: ${{ secrets.MAINPC_HOST }}
    key: ${{ secrets.MAINPC_SSH_KEY }}
    script: |
      cd /opt/gssr
      docker-compose -f docker-compose.mainpc.yml pull
      docker-compose -f docker-compose.mainpc.yml up -d --no-build
      docker run --rm --network gssr_default \
        -e DATABASE_URL=$DATABASE_URL \
        ghcr.io/pressly/goose:latest postgres "$DATABASE_URL" up
```

### Workflow 6 — deploy-zynq.yml

Trigger: after build-game (`workflow_run`)

```yaml
strategy:
  matrix:
    zynq: [zynq1, zynq2, zynq3, zynq4, zynq5]
# Docker path: ssh → docker pull + docker-compose up -d --no-build
# Bare binary fallback: scp game-server-arm, systemctl restart gssr-game
```

### Workflow 7 — test.yml

Trigger: pull_request + push to `main`

```yaml
jobs:
  test-game:
    - go test ./... -race -coverprofile=coverage.out
    - check coverage >= 80%
  test-workers:
    - pip install -r requirements.txt
    - pytest --cov=app --cov-fail-under=75
  test-frontend:
    - npm ci && npm run test -- --coverage
  e2e:
    needs: [test-game, test-workers, test-frontend]
    - docker-compose -f infra/compose/docker-compose.test.yml up -d
    - npx playwright test
    - docker-compose down
```

### Required GitHub Secrets

```text
DOCKERHUB_USERNAME / DOCKERHUB_TOKEN
CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN / CLOUDFLARE_ACCOUNT_ID
MAINPC_SSH_HOST / MAINPC_SSH_KEY
ZYNQ1_HOST … ZYNQ5_HOST
ZYNQ_SSH_KEY  (shared key for all Zynq nodes)
DATABASE_URL   (for migration step)
```

## Plan 7: Monitoring Stack (Grafana + Prometheus + Loki)

**Files:** `infra/monitoring/`

### Monitoring Services (added to docker-compose.mainpc.yml)

```yaml
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:v2.51
    volumes:
      - ./infra/monitoring/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml:ro

  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:10
    volumes:
      - grafana_data:/var/lib/grafana
      - ./infra/monitoring/grafana/provisioning:/etc/grafana/provisioning:ro
    environment:
      - GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD=${GRAFANA_PASSWORD}
      - GF_SERVER_ROOT_URL=https://grafana.school.example.com

  loki:
    image: grafana/loki:3
    volumes: [./infra/monitoring/loki.yml:/etc/loki/local-config.yaml:ro]

  promtail:
    image: grafana/promtail:3
    volumes:
      - /var/log:/var/log:ro
      - /var/lib/docker/containers:/var/lib/docker/containers:ro
      - ./infra/monitoring/promtail.yml:/etc/promtail/config.yml:ro

  cadvisor:
    image: gcr.io/cadvisor/cadvisor:v0.49
    volumes:
      - /:/rootfs:ro
      - /var/run:/var/run:ro
      - /sys:/sys:ro
      - /var/lib/docker:/var/lib/docker:ro

  node-exporter:
    image: prom/node-exporter:v1.8
    pid: host
    volumes: [/proc:/host/proc:ro, /sys:/host/sys:ro, /:/rootfs:ro]
```

### Prometheus Scrape Targets (`infra/monitoring/prometheus.yml`)

- `game:2112/metrics` — Go Fiber via `fiberprometheus`
- `workers:8000/metrics` — FastAPI via `prometheus-fastapi-instrumentator`
- `cadvisor:8080/metrics`
- `node-exporter:9100/metrics`
- `postgres-exporter:9187/metrics` (image: `prometheuscommunity/postgres-exporter`)
- `rabbitmq:15692/metrics` (rabbitmq_prometheus plugin built-in)

### Grafana Dashboards

Pre-provisioned JSON in `infra/monitoring/grafana/provisioning/dashboards/`:

- `game-engine.json` — HTTP rate, WS connections, scoring latency, Zynq node health
- `workers.json` — Celery queue depth, tiling duration, NSFW check rate
- `infra.json` — CPU/RAM per container (cAdvisor), disk I/O, PG connections
- `loki-logs.json` — Log explorer panel linked to Loki datasource

### Go Metrics Integration

```go
// cmd/server/main.go
import fiberprometheus "github.com/ansrivas/fiberprometheus/v2"

prom := fiberprometheus.New("gssr_game")
prom.RegisterAt(app, "/metrics")
app.Use(prom.Middleware)
```

### Python Metrics Integration

```python
# app/main.py
from prometheus_fastapi_instrumentator import Instrumentator
Instrumentator().instrument(app).expose(app)
```

---

## Plan 8: External Access (Cloudflare Access — Zero Trust)

Admin panel, MinIO S3 console, Grafana, and RabbitMQ management UI are exposed via
**Cloudflare Tunnel** with **Cloudflare Access policies** (no open ports required).

### Cloudflare Tunnel Routes (`infra/cloudflare/config.yml`)

```yaml
ingress:
  - hostname: game.school.example.com
    service: http://nginx:80          # public game API + WebSocket

  - hostname: admin.school.example.com
    service: http://nginx:80          # /api/admin/* → workers (Cloudflare Access protected)

  - hostname: s3.school.example.com
    service: http://minio:9001        # MinIO Console UI (Cloudflare Access protected)

  - hostname: grafana.school.example.com
    service: http://grafana:3000      # Grafana (Cloudflare Access protected)

  - hostname: mq.school.example.com
    service: http://rabbitmq:15672    # RabbitMQ management (Cloudflare Access protected)

  - service: http_status:404
```

### Cloudflare Access Policies

Configure via Cloudflare Zero Trust dashboard or Terraform (`infra/cloudflare/terraform/`):

| Application | Policy | Authentication |
| --- | --- | --- |
| admin.school.example.com | email ends with @school.example.com | One-time PIN to email OR GitHub OAuth |
| s3.school.example.com | same as admin | One-time PIN |
| grafana.school.example.com | same as admin | One-time PIN |
| mq.school.example.com | same as admin | One-time PIN |

- Free for up to 50 users on Cloudflare Zero Trust Free plan
- No VPN required: open URL → enter email → receive OTP link
- Alternative: service token (static secret `CF-Access-Client-Id` header) for automation

### Nginx Adjustments for External Routes

Admin React SPA deploys to Cloudflare Pages separately (no tunnel needed for static assets).
`admin.school.example.com` tunnel → `nginx:80` → routes `/api/admin/*` → `workers:8000`.

---

## Plan 9: k3s on Zynq Nodes (Optional — Kubernetes Orchestration)

> **When to use:** Zynq nodes run proper Linux (Debian/Ubuntu ARM), not OpenWrt.
> k3s requires ~512 MB RAM per node and cgroups v1/v2 support.
> If OpenWrt is the only option, use Docker or bare binary deployment instead.

### k3s Cluster Architecture

```text
Main PC:   k3s server (control plane) + kubectl
Zynq x5:   k3s agent (worker nodes, linux/arm/v7)
```

k3s server on Main PC (native or in Docker via `rancher/k3s`). Agents connect via LAN IP.

### k3s Setup

```bash
# Main PC — k3s server
curl -sfL https://get.k3s.io | sh -
cat /var/lib/rancher/k3s/server/node-token

# Each Zynq — k3s agent
curl -sfL https://get.k3s.io | \
  K3S_URL=https://MAINPC_IP:6443 \
  K3S_TOKEN=<node-token> \
  INSTALL_K3S_EXEC="--node-label role=game" sh -
```

### Kubernetes Manifests (`infra/k8s/`)

```text
infra/k8s/
├── namespace.yaml
├── game/
│   ├── deployment.yaml    # replicas=5, nodeAffinity: role=game
│   ├── service.yaml       # ClusterIP :3000
│   └── configmap.yaml     # env vars (non-secret)
├── kustomization.yaml
└── overlays/
    └── prod/
        └── kustomization.yaml  # image tag override per deploy
```

### Key Deployment Config

```yaml
# game/deployment.yaml (excerpt)
spec:
  replicas: 5
  strategy:
    type: RollingUpdate
    rollingUpdate: {maxUnavailable: 1, maxSurge: 1}
  template:
    spec:
      affinity:
        nodeAffinity:
          requiredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
            nodeSelectorTerms:
              - matchExpressions:
                  - {key: role, operator: In, values: [game]}
      containers:
        - name: game
          image: user/gssr-game:latest
          ports: [{containerPort: 3000}]
          livenessProbe:
            httpGet: {path: /health, port: 3000}
          readinessProbe:
            httpGet: {path: /health, port: 3000}
```

### k3s CI/CD Workflow (replaces deploy-zynq.yml)

```yaml
# .github/workflows/deploy-k3s.yml
- name: Update image tag
  run: |
    kubectl set image deployment/game \
      game=user/gssr-game:${{ github.sha }} \
      -n gssr --kubeconfig <(echo "$K3S_KUBECONFIG")
- name: Wait for rollout
  run: kubectl rollout status deployment/game -n gssr --timeout=120s
```

With k3s, Nginx upstream points to the k3s Service ClusterIP; kube-proxy handles load balancing across all 5 nodes automatically.

### Deployment Mode Decision Matrix

| Factor | Docker (per node) | Bare binary | k3s |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| RAM overhead | ~50 MB | 0 | ~300 MB/node |
| Rolling updates | manual | manual | automatic |
| Health checks | Docker healthcheck | systemd | Kubernetes probes |
| Log aggregation | Promtail per node | journald | Promtail DaemonSet |
| Complexity | low | lowest | high |
| Use when | OpenWrt + Docker | OpenWrt only | proper Linux |

---

## Implementation Order

1. **`migrations/`** — схема БД (goose SQL)
2. **`infra/`** — docker-compose + nginx + monitoring stack (локальный стенд)
3. **`services/game`** — Go Fiber: auth → rooms → WS → scoring + unit tests
4. **`services/workers`** — FastAPI + tiling + NSFW + ELO + pytest
5. **`frontend/`** — React game UI + Vitest tests
6. **`admin/`** — React admin panel + Vitest tests
7. **`e2e/`** — Playwright tests (docker-compose.test.yml)
8. **`infra/cloudflare/`** — Cloudflare Access rules (admin + s3 + grafana)
9. **`infra/k8s/`** — k3s manifests (если Zynq поддерживает)
10. **`.github/workflows/`** — CI/CD (build → test → deploy)

---

Added 1 line
Claude’s Plan
GSSR — Detailed Implementation Plan
Context
GeoGuessr School Edition: self-hosted multiplayer panorama guessing game.
Stack: Go Fiber (game engine on Zynq ARM nodes), Python FastAPI+Celery (workers on Main PC), React+Vite (frontend + admin), infra via Docker Compose, CI/CD via GitHub Actions → DockerHub.
Repo is empty — full greenfield implementation.

Monorepo Layout

gssr/
├── services/
│   ├── game/          # Go Fiber — Auth + Game Engine (Zynq nodes)
│   └── workers/       # Python FastAPI + Celery (Main PC)
├── frontend/          # React + Vite — игровой UI (Cloudflare Pages)
├── admin/             # React + Vite — Admin Panel (Cloudflare Pages)
├── infra/
│   ├── nginx/         # nginx.conf + upstream Zynq/k3s config
│   ├── compose/       # docker-compose.mainpc.yml + zynq template
│   ├── k8s/           # k3s manifests (Zynq cluster option)
│   ├── monitoring/    # Prometheus + Grafana + Loki stack
│   └── cloudflare/    # cloudflared tunnel config + Cloudflare Access rules
├── migrations/        # SQL migrations (goose)
├── .github/
│   └── workflows/
└── docs/
Plan 1: Game Engine Service (Go Fiber — Zynq nodes)
Files: services/game/

Game Service Structure

services/game/
├── cmd/server/
│   └── main.go             # entrypoint: fiber app setup, routes, graceful shutdown
├── internal/
│   ├── config/
│   │   └── config.go       # env vars via os.Getenv: VALKEY_URL, JWT_SECRET, etc.
│   ├── auth/
│   │   ├── handler.go      # POST /api/auth/register, /login, /refresh, /logout
│   │   ├── middleware.go   # JWT validation fiber middleware
│   │   └── jwt.go          # sign/verify, github.com/golang-jwt/jwt/v5
│   ├── user/
│   │   └── handler.go      # GET /api/users/me, PUT /api/users/me (avatar upload trigger)
│   ├── map/
│   │   └── handler.go      # GET /api/maps, GET /api/maps/:id (floors + panoramas list)
│   ├── room/
│   │   ├── handler.go      # POST /api/rooms, GET /api/rooms/:id, POST /api/rooms/:id/join
│   │   ├── manager.go      # in-process room registry (backed by Valkey)
│   │   └── state.go        # RoomState struct synced to Valkey JSON
│   ├── game/
│   │   ├── handler.go      # POST /api/rooms/:id/start, /guess, /next-round
│   │   └── scoring.go      # Score = Smax * exp(-(d/K)), floor mismatch → 0
│   ├── ws/
│   │   ├── hub.go          # WebSocket hub: subscribe/broadcast per room
│   │   └── handler.go      # GET /ws/rooms/:id  (gofiber/websocket)
│   ├── livekit/
│   │   └── handler.go      # POST /api/livekit/token (livekit-server-sdk-go)
│   └── db/
│       ├── postgres.go     # pgx/v5 pool, connection from POSTGRES_URL
│       └── valkey.go       # go-redis/v9 client
├── Makefile                # make build-amd64, build-arm, docker-build
├── Dockerfile              # multi-stage: golang:1.22-alpine → scratch, ARG TARGETARCH
└── go.mod
Go Dependencies

github.com/gofiber/fiber/v2
github.com/gofiber/contrib/websocket
github.com/golang-jwt/jwt/v5
github.com/redis/go-redis/v9
github.com/jackc/pgx/v5
github.com/google/uuid
github.com/livekit/server-sdk-go
github.com/ansrivas/fiberprometheus/v2
REST API Endpoints
Method	Path	Auth	Description
POST	/api/auth/register	—	create user, hash bcrypt
POST	/api/auth/login	—	return access+refresh JWT в HttpOnly cookie
POST	/api/auth/refresh	cookie	rotate refresh token
POST	/api/auth/logout	cookie	revoke refresh in Valkey
GET	/api/users/me	JWT	profile + ELO
GET	/api/maps	JWT	list all maps
GET	/api/maps/:id	JWT	map detail + floors + panorama count
POST	/api/rooms	JWT	create room (map_id, max_players, rounds)
GET	/api/rooms/:id	JWT	room state
POST	/api/rooms/:id/join	JWT	join room
POST	/api/rooms/:id/start	JWT (host)	start game
POST	/api/rooms/:id/guess	JWT	submit guess {pano_id, x, y, floor_id}
GET	/api/rooms/:id/results	JWT	round/game results
POST	/api/livekit/token	JWT	generate LK access token for room
WebSocket Events (/ws/rooms/:id)

server → client:
  player_joined   { user_id, username, avatar }
  player_left     { user_id }
  round_started   { round, pano_id, time_limit_sec }
  guess_broadcast { user_id, x, y, floor_id }   (after all guessed or timeout)
  round_ended     { scores: [{user_id, score, distance}], correct: {x,y,floor} }
  game_ended      { leaderboard: [{user_id, total_score, elo_delta}] }

client → server:
  ping / pong
Scoring Logic (internal/game/scoring.go)

const Smax = 5000.0
func CalculateScore(gx, gy, ax, ay float64, gFloor, aFloor int, K float64) int {
    if gFloor != aFloor { return 0 }
    d := math.Sqrt(math.Pow(gx-ax, 2) + math.Pow(gy-ay, 2))
    return int(Smax * math.Exp(-(d / K)))
}
Game Service Tests

internal/
  auth/handler_test.go      # httptest: register, login, token rotation
  game/scoring_test.go      # table-driven unit tests for CalculateScore
  room/manager_test.go      # room state sync to Valkey (testcontainers-go Redis)
  ws/hub_test.go            # goroutine hub: broadcast, disconnect
integration/
  auth_integration_test.go  # full flow with real PG (testcontainers-go Postgres)
  game_integration_test.go  # create room → join → guess → score
Key tools: testcontainers-go, net/http/httptest, github.com/stretchr/testify

Makefile targets: make test (go test ./... -race), make test-coverage (threshold 80%)

Game Service Deployment
Docker (preferred): docker pull user/gssr-game:latest → docker run --env-file .env
Bare binary: make build-arm → CGO_ENABLED=0 GOOS=linux GOARCH=arm GOARM=7 go build → SCP + systemd
k3s (see Plan 9)
Plan 2: Worker Service (Python FastAPI + Celery — Main PC)
Files: services/workers/

Worker Service Structure

services/workers/
├── app/
│   ├── main.py              # FastAPI app, mounts routers, CORS (admin only)
│   ├── config.py            # pydantic-settings: PG URL, MinIO, RabbitMQ, etc.
│   ├── api/
│   │   ├── admin_maps.py    # POST /admin/maps, /maps/:id/floors
│   │   ├── admin_panos.py   # POST /admin/panoramas, GET /pending, approve/reject
│   │   ├── admin_users.py   # GET /admin/users, PUT /admin/users/:id/ban
│   │   └── health.py        # GET /health, GET /metrics
│   ├── tasks/
│   │   ├── celery_app.py    # Celery instance, broker=rabbitmq, backend=valkey
│   │   ├── tiling.py        # tile_panorama(pano_id): pyvips DeepZoom → MinIO
│   │   ├── moderation.py    # moderate_panorama(pano_id): onnxruntime NSFW inference
│   │   └── elo.py           # recalculate_elo(match_id): consume RabbitMQ event
│   ├── db/
│   │   ├── base.py          # SQLAlchemy async engine
│   │   └── models.py        # ORM models mirroring SQL schema
│   └── storage/
│       └── minio_client.py  # boto3 S3 client wrapper
├── celery_worker.py         # entrypoint: celery -A app.tasks.celery_app worker
├── Dockerfile
├── requirements.txt
└── pyproject.toml
Python Dependencies

fastapi uvicorn[standard]
celery[librabbitmq]
sqlalchemy[asyncio] asyncpg
pyvips                # libvips Python bindings (apt: libvips-dev)
boto3                 # MinIO S3
onnxruntime           # NSFW model inference
Pillow
pika                  # RabbitMQ consumer for ELO
pydantic-settings
prometheus-fastapi-instrumentator
Admin REST API
Method	Path	Description
POST	/admin/maps	create map (name, x_min, x_max, y_min, y_max)
POST	/admin/maps/:id/floors	upload floor image → MinIO, create Floor record
POST	/admin/panoramas	upload equirectangular JPEG/PNG → trigger tiling + moderation tasks
GET	/admin/panoramas/pending	moderation queue (NSFW flagged or manual review)
POST	/admin/panoramas/:id/approve	set status=published
POST	/admin/panoramas/:id/reject	set status=rejected + delete tiles from MinIO
GET	/admin/users	paginated user list
PUT	/admin/users/:id/ban	set banned=true
GET	/admin/stats	total maps/panos/players/matches
Celery Task Flow

upload panorama
    → tile_panorama.delay(pano_id)
          libvips.Image.dzsave() → DeepZoom tiles
          upload to MinIO: /maps/{map_id}/panoramas/{pano_id}/{level}/{x}_{y}.webp
          update DB: pano.tile_status = "tiled"
    → moderate_panorama.delay(pano_id)  [parallel]
          onnxruntime NSFW model → score
          if score > threshold: pano.moderation = "flagged"
          else: pano.moderation = "clean"

match end event (RabbitMQ)
    → recalculate_elo(match_id)
          fetch match results, Elo formula per player
          UPDATE users SET elo = ...
MinIO Path Convention

/maps/{map_id}/floors/{floor_id}.webp
/maps/{map_id}/panoramas/{pano_id}/{zoom_level}/{col}_{row}.webp
/avatars/{user_id}.webp
Worker Service Tests

tests/
  test_api_maps.py         # pytest + httpx AsyncClient: create map, upload floor
  test_api_panos.py        # upload panorama → check task queued
  test_tasks_tiling.py     # mock pyvips + minio: tile_panorama task completes
  test_tasks_moderation.py # mock onnxruntime: score above/below threshold
  test_elo.py              # ELO formula unit tests with known inputs
conftest.py                # pytest fixtures: async engine, test DB (testcontainers), minio mock
Key tools: pytest, pytest-asyncio, httpx, factory_boy, testcontainers[postgres], moto (S3 mock)

Note: Marzipano used as UMD via <script> tag or ESM import from npm.

Game Flow (Game.tsx state machine)

WAITING → ROUND_ACTIVE → GUESSING → ROUND_RESULTS → (next round / GAME_OVER)

ROUND_ACTIVE:
  - PanoramaViewer shows current panorama tiles
  - GuessMap allows placing pin
  - FloorSelector for multi-floor maps
  - Timer countdown
  - VoiceChat always visible

GUESSING (after submit or timeout):
  - GuessMap shows all players' pins
  - correct location revealed

ROUND_RESULTS:
  - ScoreBoard with distances + scores
  - Transition to next round after N seconds
Frontend Tests

src/__tests__/
  scoring.test.ts            # pure CalculateScore util (identical formula in TS)
  useGameState.test.ts       # Vitest: zustand store transitions
  GuessMap.test.tsx          # React Testing Library: click places pin
  PanoramaViewer.test.tsx    # mock Marzipano, verify tile URL constructed correctly
  ScoreBoard.test.tsx        # renders correct scores and distances
  nsfwCheck.test.ts          # mock nsfwjs, verify above/below threshold behavior
e2e/
  auth.spec.ts               # Playwright: register → login → profile page
  game.spec.ts               # create room → start game → submit guess → see score
  admin.spec.ts              # upload panorama → appears in moderation queue
Key tools: vitest, @testing-library/react, msw (mock API), playwright

Plan 5: Infrastructure (Main PC — Docker Compose + Nginx)
Files: infra/

docker-compose.mainpc.yml

services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:16-alpine
    volumes: [pgdata:/var/lib/postgresql/data]
    env: POSTGRES_DB, POSTGRES_USER, POSTGRES_PASSWORD

  valkey:
    image: valkey/valkey:7-alpine
    command: valkey-server --save 60 1

  rabbitmq:
    image: rabbitmq:3.13-management-alpine

  minio:
    image: minio/minio:latest
    command: server /data --console-address ":9001"
    volumes: [minio_data:/data]
    env: MINIO_ROOT_USER, MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD

  workers:
    image: user/gssr-workers:latest
    depends_on: [postgres, valkey, rabbitmq, minio]
    env_file: .env.workers

  celery:
    image: user/gssr-workers:latest
    command: celery -A app.tasks.celery_app worker -l info -Q default
    depends_on: [rabbitmq, valkey]
    env_file: .env.workers

  livekit:
    image: livekit/livekit-server:latest
    command: --config /etc/livekit.yaml
    volumes: [./livekit.yaml:/etc/livekit.yaml]

  nginx:
    image: nginx:1.27-alpine
    volumes:
      - ./infra/nginx/nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf:ro
    ports: [80, 443]

  cloudflared:
    image: cloudflare/cloudflared:latest
    command: tunnel --config /etc/cf/config.yml run
    volumes: [./infra/cloudflare:/etc/cf:ro]

  portainer:
    image: portainer/portainer-ce:latest
    volumes:
      - /var/run/docker.sock:/var/run/docker.sock
      - portainer_data:/data
    restart: unless-stopped
    # exposed via cloudflared as portainer.school.example.com (Cloudflare Access protected)
Nginx Routing (infra/nginx/nginx.conf)

upstream zynq_game {
    least_conn;
    server zynq1:3000;
    server zynq2:3000;
    server zynq3:3000;
    server zynq4:3000;
    server zynq5:3000;
}

# /api/* → Zynq round-robin (except /api/admin/*)
# /api/admin/* → workers:8000
# /ws/* → Zynq (upgrade: WebSocket)
# /s3/* → minio:9000 (proxy pass, strip prefix)
# /livekit/* → livekit:7880
Database Migrations (migrations/)
Using goose (SQL-based, no ORM lock-in):


migrations/
├── 00001_create_users.sql
├── 00002_create_maps.sql
├── 00003_create_floors.sql
├── 00004_create_panoramas.sql
├── 00005_create_matches.sql
└── 00006_create_guesses.sql
Key schema:


-- users: id, username, password_hash, avatar_url, elo, banned, created_at
-- maps: id, name, x_min, x_max, y_min, y_max, coord_type
-- floors: id, map_id, floor_number, image_url
-- panoramas: id, floor_id, x, y, north_offset, tile_status, moderation_status
-- matches: id, room_id, map_id, started_at, ended_at
-- guesses: id, match_id, user_id, panorama_id, guess_x, guess_y, guess_floor_id, score
Zynq Docker Compose (infra/compose/docker-compose.zynq.yml)

services:
  game:
    image: user/gssr-game:latest
    platform: linux/arm/v7
    env_file: .env.zynq
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports: [3000:3000]
Bare binary alternative: infra/zynq/deploy.sh — SCP binary + restart systemd unit.

Plan 6: CI/CD (GitHub Actions + DockerHub)
Files: .github/workflows/

Workflow 1 — build-game.yml
Trigger: push to main or tag game/v*


- name: Set up QEMU        # for arm/v7 emulation
- name: Set up buildx
- name: Login to DockerHub
- name: Build & push
  uses: docker/build-push-action
  with:
    context: services/game
    platforms: linux/amd64,linux/arm/v7
    tags: user/gssr-game:latest,user/gssr-game:${{ github.sha }}
    cache-from: type=gha
    cache-to: type=gha,mode=max
Workflow 2 — build-workers.yml
Trigger: push to main or tag workers/v*

Same structure, single platform linux/amd64.

Workflow 3 — deploy-frontend.yml
Trigger: push to main, path frontend/**


- run: npm ci && npm run build
- uses: cloudflare/wrangler-action
  with:
    command: pages deploy dist --project-name=gssr-frontend
Workflow 4 — deploy-admin.yml
Same as Workflow 3, path admin/**, project-name=gssr-admin.

Workflow 5 — deploy-mainpc.yml
Trigger: after build-game + build-workers complete (workflow_run)


- name: Deploy via SSH
  uses: appleboy/ssh-action
  with:
    host: ${{ secrets.MAINPC_HOST }}
    key: ${{ secrets.MAINPC_SSH_KEY }}
    script: |
      cd /opt/gssr
      docker-compose -f docker-compose.mainpc.yml pull
      docker-compose -f docker-compose.mainpc.yml up -d --no-build
      docker run --rm --network gssr_default \
        -e DATABASE_URL=$DATABASE_URL \
        ghcr.io/pressly/goose:latest postgres "$DATABASE_URL" up
Workflow 6 — deploy-zynq.yml
Trigger: after build-game (workflow_run)


strategy:
  matrix:
    zynq: [zynq1, zynq2, zynq3, zynq4, zynq5]
# Docker path: ssh → docker pull + docker-compose up -d --no-build
# Bare binary fallback: scp game-server-arm, systemctl restart gssr-game
Workflow 7 — test.yml
Trigger: pull_request + push to main


jobs:
  test-game:
    - go test ./... -race -coverprofile=coverage.out
    - check coverage >= 80%
  test-workers:
    - pip install -r requirements.txt
    - pytest --cov=app --cov-fail-under=75
  test-frontend:
    - npm ci && npm run test -- --coverage
  e2e:
    needs: [test-game, test-workers, test-frontend]
    - docker-compose -f infra/compose/docker-compose.test.yml up -d
    - npx playwright test
    - docker-compose down
Required GitHub Secrets

DOCKERHUB_USERNAME / DOCKERHUB_TOKEN
CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN / CLOUDFLARE_ACCOUNT_ID
MAINPC_SSH_HOST / MAINPC_SSH_KEY
ZYNQ1_HOST … ZYNQ5_HOST
ZYNQ_SSH_KEY  (shared key for all Zynq nodes)
DATABASE_URL   (for migration step)
Plan 7: Monitoring Stack (Grafana + Prometheus + Loki)
Files: infra/monitoring/

Monitoring Services (added to docker-compose.mainpc.yml)

  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:v2.51
    volumes:
      - ./infra/monitoring/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml:ro

  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:10
    volumes:
      - grafana_data:/var/lib/grafana
      - ./infra/monitoring/grafana/provisioning:/etc/grafana/provisioning:ro
    environment:
      - GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD=${GRAFANA_PASSWORD}
      - GF_SERVER_ROOT_URL=https://grafana.school.example.com

  loki:
    image: grafana/loki:3
    volumes: [./infra/monitoring/loki.yml:/etc/loki/local-config.yaml:ro]

  promtail:
    image: grafana/promtail:3
    volumes:
      - /var/log:/var/log:ro
      - /var/lib/docker/containers:/var/lib/docker/containers:ro
      - ./infra/monitoring/promtail.yml:/etc/promtail/config.yml:ro

  cadvisor:
    image: gcr.io/cadvisor/cadvisor:v0.49
    volumes:
      - /:/rootfs:ro
      - /var/run:/var/run:ro
      - /sys:/sys:ro
      - /var/lib/docker:/var/lib/docker:ro

  node-exporter:
    image: prom/node-exporter:v1.8
    pid: host
    volumes: [/proc:/host/proc:ro, /sys:/host/sys:ro, /:/rootfs:ro]
Prometheus Scrape Targets (infra/monitoring/prometheus.yml)

workers:8000/metrics — FastAPI via prometheus-fastapi-instrumentator
cadvisor:8080/metrics

Grafana Dashboards

workers.json — Celery queue depth, tiling duration, NSFW check rate
infra.json — CPU/RAM per container (cAdvisor), disk I/O, PG connections
loki-logs.json — Log explorer panel linked to Loki datasource
Go Metrics Integration

// cmd/server/main.go
import fiberprometheus "github.com/ansrivas/fiberprometheus/v2"

prom := fiberprometheus.New("gssr_game")
prom.RegisterAt(app, "/metrics")
app.Use(prom.Middleware)
Python Metrics Integration

# app/main.py
from prometheus_fastapi_instrumentator import Instrumentator
Instrumentator().instrument(app).expose(app)
Plan 8: External Access (Cloudflare Access — Zero Trust)
Admin panel, MinIO S3 console, Grafana, and RabbitMQ management UI are exposed via
Cloudflare Tunnel with Cloudflare Access policies (no open ports required).

Cloudflare Tunnel Routes (infra/cloudflare/config.yml)

ingress:
  - hostname: game.school.example.com
    service: http://nginx:80          # public game API + WebSocket

  - hostname: admin.school.example.com
    service: http://nginx:80          # /api/admin/* → workers (Cloudflare Access protected)

  - hostname: s3.school.example.com
    service: http://minio:9001        # MinIO Console UI (Cloudflare Access protected)

  - hostname: grafana.school.example.com
    service: http://grafana:3000      # Grafana (Cloudflare Access protected)

  - hostname: mq.school.example.com
    service: http://rabbitmq:15672    # RabbitMQ management (Cloudflare Access protected)

  - hostname: portainer.school.example.com
    service: http://portainer:9000    # Portainer Docker UI (Cloudflare Access protected)

  - service: http_status:404
Cloudflare Access Policies
Configure via Cloudflare Zero Trust dashboard or Terraform (infra/cloudflare/terraform/):

Application	Policy	Authentication
admin.school.example.com	email ends with @school.example.com	One-time PIN to email OR GitHub OAuth
s3.school.example.com	same as admin	One-time PIN
grafana.school.example.com	same as admin	One-time PIN
mq.school.example.com	same as admin	One-time PIN
portainer.school.example.com	same as admin	One-time PIN
Free for up to 50 users on Cloudflare Zero Trust Free plan
No VPN required: open URL → enter email → receive OTP link
Alternative: service token (static secret CF-Access-Client-Id header) for automation
Nginx Adjustments for External Routes
Admin React SPA deploys to Cloudflare Pages separately (no tunnel needed for static assets).
admin.school.example.com tunnel → nginx:80 → routes /api/admin/* → workers:8000.

Plan 9: k3s on Zynq Nodes (Optional — Kubernetes Orchestration)
When to use: Zynq nodes run proper Linux (Debian/Ubuntu ARM), not OpenWrt.
k3s requires ~512 MB RAM per node and cgroups v1/v2 support.
If OpenWrt is the only option, use Docker or bare binary deployment instead.

k3s Cluster Architecture

Main PC:   k3s server (control plane) + kubectl
Zynq x5:   k3s agent (worker nodes, linux/arm/v7)
k3s server on Main PC (native or in Docker via rancher/k3s). Agents connect via LAN IP.

k3s Setup

# Main PC — k3s server
curl -sfL https://get.k3s.io | sh -
cat /var/lib/rancher/k3s/server/node-token

# Each Zynq — k3s agent
curl -sfL https://get.k3s.io | \
  K3S_URL=https://MAINPC_IP:6443 \
  K3S_TOKEN=<node-token> \
  INSTALL_K3S_EXEC="--node-label role=game" sh -
Kubernetes Manifests (infra/k8s/)

infra/k8s/
├── namespace.yaml
├── game/
│   ├── deployment.yaml    # replicas=5, nodeAffinity: role=game
│   ├── service.yaml       # ClusterIP :3000
│   └── configmap.yaml     # env vars (non-secret)
├── kustomization.yaml
└── overlays/
    └── prod/
        └── kustomization.yaml  # image tag override per deploy
Key Deployment Config

# game/deployment.yaml (excerpt)
spec:
  replicas: 5
  strategy:
    type: RollingUpdate
    rollingUpdate: {maxUnavailable: 1, maxSurge: 1}
  template:
    spec:
      affinity:
        nodeAffinity:
          requiredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
            nodeSelectorTerms:
              - matchExpressions:
                  - {key: role, operator: In, values: [game]}
      containers:
        - name: game
          image: user/gssr-game:latest
          ports: [{containerPort: 3000}]
          livenessProbe:
            httpGet: {path: /health, port: 3000}
          readinessProbe:
            httpGet: {path: /health, port: 3000}
k3s CI/CD Workflow (replaces deploy-zynq.yml)

# .github/workflows/deploy-k3s.yml
- name: Update image tag
  run: |
    kubectl set image deployment/game \
      game=user/gssr-game:${{ github.sha }} \
      -n gssr --kubeconfig <(echo "$K3S_KUBECONFIG")
- name: Wait for rollout
  run: kubectl rollout status deployment/game -n gssr --timeout=120s
With k3s, Nginx upstream points to the k3s Service ClusterIP; kube-proxy handles load balancing across all 5 nodes automatically.

Deployment Mode Decision Matrix
Factor	Docker (per node)	Bare binary	k3s
RAM overhead	~50 MB	0	~300 MB/node
Rolling updates	manual	manual	automatic
Health checks	Docker healthcheck	systemd	Kubernetes probes
Log aggregation	Promtail per node	journald	Promtail DaemonSet
Complexity	low	lowest	high
Use when	OpenWrt + Docker	OpenWrt only	proper Linux
Plan 10: Documentation in Repository (docs/)
The architecture plan is split into step-by-step implementation guides living in the repo.
Each file corresponds to one implementation step and can be followed independently.

Documentation Structure

docs/
├── arch-plan.md              # existing high-level architecture overview (keep)
├── steps/
│   ├── 01-migrations.md      # DB schema setup with goose: how to run, table descriptions
│   ├── 02-infra-local.md     # docker-compose up on Main PC: env vars, health checks, first run
│   ├── 03-game-service.md    # Go Fiber service: structure, building, running locally, env vars
│   ├── 04-worker-service.md  # Python FastAPI + Celery: setup, libvips install, NSFW model download
│   ├── 05-frontend.md        # React game UI: local dev, Marzipano setup, env vars
│   ├── 06-admin-panel.md     # React admin UI: upload flow, moderation queue walkthrough
│   ├── 07-testing.md         # Running all tests: Go, Python, Vitest, Playwright E2E
│   ├── 08-cloudflare.md      # Tunnel setup, Access policies, DNS records
│   ├── 09-monitoring.md      # Prometheus + Grafana + Loki: importing dashboards, alert rules
│   ├── 10-cicd.md            # GitHub Actions secrets, workflow triggers, DockerHub setup
│   ├── 11-zynq-docker.md     # Deploying game service to Zynq nodes via Docker or bare binary
│   └── 12-k3s.md             # Optional: k3s cluster setup, kubectl, kustomize deploy
Content Convention for Each Step File
Each docs/steps/NN-name.md follows the same structure:


# Step N: Title

## Goal
One sentence describing what this step achieves.

## Prerequisites
- Previous steps completed
- Required env vars / secrets

## Steps
1. ...
2. ...

## Verification
How to confirm this step is complete (curl, docker ps, UI check).

## Troubleshooting
Common errors and fixes.
The plan file (this file) is the source of truth for architecture decisions.
The docs/steps/ files are operational runbooks for actually doing the work.

Implementation Order
migrations/ — схема БД (goose SQL) → docs/steps/01-migrations.md
infra/ — docker-compose + nginx + monitoring + Portainer → docs/steps/02-infra-local.md
services/game — Go Fiber: auth → rooms → WS → scoring + unit tests → docs/steps/03-game-service.md
services/workers — FastAPI + tiling + NSFW + ELO + pytest → docs/steps/04-worker-service.md
frontend/ — React game UI + Vitest tests → docs/steps/05-frontend.md
admin/ — React admin panel + Vitest tests → docs/steps/06-admin-panel.md
e2e/ — Playwright tests → docs/steps/07-testing.md
infra/cloudflare/ — Cloudflare tunnel + Access (admin, s3, grafana, portainer, mq) → docs/steps/08-cloudflare.md
infra/monitoring/ — Grafana dashboards provisioning → docs/steps/09-monitoring.md
.github/workflows/ — CI/CD → docs/steps/10-cicd.md
infra/zynq/ — Zynq deploy (Docker or bare binary) → docs/steps/11-zynq-docker.md
infra/k8s/ — k3s manifests (если Zynq поддерживает) → docs/steps/12-k3s.md
Verification / Testing Checklist
docker-compose up -d на Main PC → все сервисы healthy
goose up → миграции применились, schema корректна
Game Engine: curl -X POST /api/auth/register → JWT cookie returned
Game Engine: создать room, join 2 игрока, WebSocket events приходят
Workers: загрузить 8K панораму → тайлы появились в MinIO bucket
Workers: NSFW сцена → статус flagged, чистое фото → clean
Grafana: открыть https://grafana.school.example.com → Cloudflare Access prompt → dashboards loaded
MinIO: открыть https://s3.school.example.com → Cloudflare Access prompt → console loaded
Portainer: открыть https://portainer.school.example.com → Cloudflare Access → все контейнеры видны
Frontend: Marzipano рендерит тайлы, Leaflet принимает клик → очки считаются
CI: push в main → DockerHub образ пересобирается → Main PC деплоится автоматически
Zynq: docker pull нового образа ИЛИ SCP бинаря → сервис рестартует без даунтайма

Write 01-migrations.md
