Write tiling.py
77 lines
import os
import tempfile
import logging
from pathlib import Path

import pyvips

from app.tasks.celery_app import celery_app
from app.config import settings
from app.storage.minio_client import minio_client

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


@celery_app.task(name="tile_panorama", bind=True, max_retries=3)
def tile_panorama(self, pano_id: str):
    """Download raw panorama from MinIO, generate DeepZoom tiles, upload back."""
    from app.db.base import sync_engine
    from sqlalchemy import text

    logger.info("Tiling panorama %s", pano_id)

    # Update status to "tiling"
    with sync_engine.begin() as conn:
        conn.execute(
            text("UPDATE panoramas SET tile_status = 'tiling' WHERE id = :id"),
            {"id": pano_id},
        )

    try:
        raw_key = f"raw/{pano_id}.jpg"
        with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmpdir:
            raw_path = os.path.join(tmpdir, "panorama.jpg")

            # Download original
            minio_client.fget_object(settings.minio_bucket, raw_key, raw_path)

            # Generate DeepZoom tiles
            out_dir = os.path.join(tmpdir, "tiles")
            img = pyvips.Image.new_from_file(raw_path, access="sequential")
            img.dzsave(
                out_dir,
                layout="google",
                tile_size=256,
                overlap=0,
                suffix=".webp[Q=85]",
                depth="onetile",
            )

            # Upload tile tree to MinIO
            prefix = f"maps/panoramas/{pano_id}"
            for root, _, files in os.walk(out_dir):
                for fname in files:
                    local_path = os.path.join(root, fname)
                    rel = os.path.relpath(local_path, out_dir)
                    minio_key = f"{prefix}/{rel}".replace("\\", "/")
                    minio_client.fput_object(
                        settings.minio_bucket, minio_key, local_path
                    )

        # Mark as tiled
        with sync_engine.begin() as conn:
            conn.execute(
                text("UPDATE panoramas SET tile_status = 'tiled' WHERE id = :id"),
                {"id": pano_id},
            )
        logger.info("Tiling complete for %s", pano_id)

    except Exception as exc:
        logger.error("Tiling failed for %s: %s", pano_id, exc)
        with sync_engine.begin() as conn:
            conn.execute(
                text("UPDATE panoramas SET tile_status = 'failed' WHERE id = :id"),
                {"id": pano_id},
            )
        raise self.retry(exc=exc, countdown=60)
Write moderation.py
75 lines
import logging
import tempfile
import os

import numpy as np
import onnxruntime as rt
from PIL import Image

from app.tasks.celery_app import celery_app
from app.config import settings
from app.storage.minio_client import minio_client

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

_session = None


def _get_session():
    global _session
    if _session is None:
        _session = rt.InferenceSession(settings.nsfw_model_path)
    return _session


def _preprocess(img_path: str) -> np.ndarray:
    """Resize to 299×299, normalize to [-1, 1], add batch dim."""
    img = Image.open(img_path).convert("RGB").resize((299, 299))
    arr = np.array(img, dtype=np.float32) / 127.5 - 1.0
    return np.expand_dims(arr, axis=0)


@celery_app.task(name="moderate_panorama", bind=True, max_retries=2)
def moderate_panorama(self, pano_id: str):
    """Run NSFW detection on a panorama's raw image."""
    from app.db.base import sync_engine
    from sqlalchemy import text

    logger.info("Moderating panorama %s", pano_id)

    try:
        raw_key = f"raw/{pano_id}.jpg"
        with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(suffix=".jpg", delete=False) as f:
            tmp_path = f.name

        minio_client.fget_object(settings.minio_bucket, raw_key, tmp_path)

        session = _get_session()
        input_name = session.get_inputs()[0].name
        tensor = _preprocess(tmp_path)
        outputs = session.run(None, {input_name: tensor})
        # Expected output: [[drawings, hentai, neutral, porn, sexy]]
        scores = outputs[0][0]
        classes = ["drawings", "hentai", "neutral", "porn", "sexy"]
        result = dict(zip(classes, scores.tolist()))
        nsfw_score = result.get("porn", 0) + result.get("hentai", 0)

        os.unlink(tmp_path)

        status = "flagged" if nsfw_score > settings.nsfw_threshold else "clean"
        logger.info("Panorama %s moderation: %s (score=%.3f)", pano_id, status, nsfw_score)

        with sync_engine.begin() as conn:
            conn.execute(
                text("""
                    UPDATE panoramas
                    SET moderation_status = :status, nsfw_score = :score
                    WHERE id = :id
                """),
                {"status": status, "score": float(nsfw_score), "id": pano_id},
            )

    except Exception as exc:
        logger.error("Moderation failed for %s: %s", pano_id, exc)
        raise self.retry(exc=exc, countdown=30)
Write elo.py
76 lines
import logging
from app.tasks.celery_app import celery_app

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

K_NEW = 32    # < 30 matches
K_EXP = 16   # >= 30 matches
ELO_DIVISOR = 400.0


def expected_score(rating_a: float, rating_b: float) -> float:
    return 1.0 / (1.0 + 10 ** ((rating_b - rating_a) / ELO_DIVISOR))


def new_elo(rating: float, actual: float, expected: float, k: int) -> int:
    return round(rating + k * (actual - expected))


@celery_app.task(name="recalculate_elo")
def recalculate_elo(match_id: str):
    """
    Recalculate ELO ratings for all players in a finished match.
    Called after a match ends (triggered via RabbitMQ or direct Celery call).
    """
    from app.db.base import sync_engine
    from sqlalchemy import text

    logger.info("Recalculating ELO for match %s", match_id)

    with sync_engine.begin() as conn:
        rows = conn.execute(
            text("""
                SELECT g.user_id, SUM(g.score) as total_score, u.elo,
                       COUNT(DISTINCT m2.id) as match_count
                FROM guesses g
                JOIN users u ON u.id = g.user_id
                LEFT JOIN guesses m2 ON m2.user_id = g.user_id
                WHERE g.match_id = :match_id
                GROUP BY g.user_id, u.elo
                ORDER BY total_score DESC
            """),
            {"match_id": match_id},
        ).fetchall()

    if len(rows) < 2:
        return

    # Sort by score descending (already sorted)
    # Pairwise ELO: each player vs average of others
    player_elos = {str(r.user_id): r.elo for r in rows}
    player_scores = {str(r.user_id): r.total_score for r in rows}
    player_matches = {str(r.user_id): r.match_count for r in rows}

    max_score = max(player_scores.values()) or 1
    new_elos = {}

    for uid, elo in player_elos.items():
        k = K_NEW if player_matches[uid] < 30 else K_EXP
        # Actual = normalized score position
        rank = sorted(player_scores.values(), reverse=True).index(player_scores[uid])
        actual = 1.0 - (rank / (len(rows) - 1))
        avg_opponent_elo = sum(
            v for k2, v in player_elos.items() if k2 != uid
        ) / max(len(player_elos) - 1, 1)
        exp = expected_score(elo, avg_opponent_elo)
        new_elos[uid] = new_elo(elo, actual, exp, k)

    with sync_engine.begin() as conn:
        for uid, elo in new_elos.items():
            conn.execute(
                text("UPDATE users SET elo = :elo WHERE id = :id"),
                {"elo": elo, "id": uid},
            )

    logger.info("ELO updated for match %s: %s", match_id, new_elos)

from minio import Minio
from app.config import settings

    settings.minio_endpoint,

    secret_key=settings.minio_secret_key,

)


def ensure_bucket():
    if not minio_client.bucket_exists(settings.minio_bucket):
        minio_client.make_bucket(settings.minio_bucket)
        # Set public read policy for tiles
        policy = f'''{{
            "Version": "2012-10-17",
            "Statement": [{{
                "Effect": "Allow",
                "Principal": {{"AWS": ["*"]}},
                "Action": ["s3:GetObject"],
                "Resource": ["arn:aws:s3:::{settings.minio_bucket}/maps/*"]
            }}]
        }}'''
        minio_client.set_bucket_policy(settings.minio_bucket, policy)

Write test_elo.py
39 lines
import pytest
from app.tasks.elo import expected_score, new_elo, K_NEW, K_EXP


def test_expected_score_equal_ratings():
    assert abs(expected_score(1000, 1000) - 0.5) < 0.001


def test_expected_score_higher_rating():
    # Higher rated player should have > 0.5 expected score
    assert expected_score(1200, 1000) > 0.5


def test_expected_score_lower_rating():
    assert expected_score(800, 1000) < 0.5


def test_new_elo_win_increases():
    # If player wins (actual=1) vs expected (0.5), rating should increase
    result = new_elo(1000, 1.0, 0.5, K_NEW)
    assert result > 1000


def test_new_elo_loss_decreases():
    result = new_elo(1000, 0.0, 0.5, K_NEW)
    assert result < 1000


def test_new_elo_draw_unchanged():
    result = new_elo(1000, 0.5, 0.5, K_NEW)
    assert result == 1000


def test_k_factor_new_player():
    # New players (K=32) should have bigger swings
    gain_new = new_elo(1000, 1.0, 0.5, K_NEW) - 1000
    gain_exp = new_elo(1000, 1.0, 0.5, K_EXP) - 1000
    assert gain_new > gain_exp

Write client.ts

import axios from 'axios'

const client = axios.create({
  baseURL: import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL || '',
  withCredentials: true, // include HttpOnly cookies
})

// Refresh token on 401
client.interceptors.response.use(
  (r) => r,
  async (error) => {
    if (error.response?.status === 401 && !error.config._retry) {
      error.config._retry = true
      try {
        await client.post('/api/auth/refresh')
        return client(error.config)
      } catch {
        window.location.href = '/login'
      }
    }
    return Promise.reject(error)
  }
)

export default client
Write gameStore.ts
89 lines
import { create } from 'zustand'

export type GameStatus = 'waiting' | 'round_active' | 'guessing' | 'round_results' | 'game_over'

export interface Player {
  userId: string
  username: string
  avatarUrl?: string
  elo: number
  hasGuessed: boolean
}

export interface RoundResult {
  userId: string
  score: number
  distance: number
}

export interface Guess {
  x: number
  y: number
  floorId: string
}

interface GameState {
  roomId: string | null
  mapId: string | null
  status: GameStatus
  players: Player[]
  currentRound: number
  totalRounds: number
  currentPanoId: string | null
  myGuess: Guess | null
  roundResults: RoundResult[]
  timeLimitSec: number
  correctLocation: { x: number; y: number; floorId: string } | null

  setRoom: (roomId: string, mapId: string) => void
  setStatus: (status: GameStatus) => void
  setPlayers: (players: Player[]) => void
  addPlayer: (player: Player) => void
  removePlayer: (userId: string) => void
  setPlayerGuessed: (userId: string) => void
  startRound: (round: number, panoId: string, timeLimitSec: number) => void
  setMyGuess: (guess: Guess) => void
  setRoundResults: (results: RoundResult[], correct: GameState['correctLocation']) => void
  reset: () => void
}

export const useGameStore = create<GameState>((set) => ({
  roomId: null,
  mapId: null,
  status: 'waiting',
  players: [],
  currentRound: 0,
  totalRounds: 5,
  currentPanoId: null,
  myGuess: null,
  roundResults: [],
  timeLimitSec: 60,
  correctLocation: null,

  setRoom: (roomId, mapId) => set({ roomId, mapId }),
  setStatus: (status) => set({ status }),
  setPlayers: (players) => set({ players }),
  addPlayer: (player) => set((s) => ({ players: [...s.players, player] })),
  removePlayer: (userId) => set((s) => ({ players: s.players.filter((p) => p.userId !== userId) })),
  setPlayerGuessed: (userId) =>
    set((s) => ({
      players: s.players.map((p) => (p.userId === userId ? { ...p, hasGuessed: true } : p)),
    })),
  startRound: (round, panoId, timeLimitSec) =>
    set({ currentRound: round, currentPanoId: panoId, timeLimitSec, myGuess: null, status: 'round_active' }),
  setMyGuess: (guess) => set({ myGuess: guess }),
  setRoundResults: (roundResults, correctLocation) =>
    set({ roundResults, correctLocation, status: 'round_results' }),
  reset: () =>
    set({
      roomId: null,
      mapId: null,
      status: 'waiting',
      players: [],
      currentRound: 0,
      currentPanoId: null,
      myGuess: null,
      roundResults: [],
    }),
}))
Write nsfwCheck.ts
27 lines
import * as nsfwjs from 'nsfwjs'

let model: nsfwjs.NSFWJS | null = null

async function getModel(): Promise<nsfwjs.NSFWJS> {
  if (!model) {
    model = await nsfwjs.load()
  }
  return model
}

const NSFW_CLASSES = ['Porn', 'Hentai', 'Sexy']
const NSFW_THRESHOLD = 0.7

/**
 * Returns true if the image is likely NSFW.
 * @param imgElement - An HTMLImageElement to classify
 */
export async function isNSFW(imgElement: HTMLImageElement): Promise<boolean> {
  const m = await getModel()
  const predictions = await m.classify(imgElement)
  const nsfwScore = predictions
    .filter((p) => NSFW_CLASSES.includes(p.className))
    .reduce((sum, p) => sum + p.probability, 0)
  return nsfwScore > NSFW_THRESHOLD
}
Write useWebSocket.ts
87 lines
import { useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react'
import { useGameStore } from '../store/gameStore'

type WSMessage = { event: string; payload?: unknown }

const RECONNECT_BASE_MS = 1000
const RECONNECT_MAX_MS = 30000

export function useWebSocket(roomId: string | null) {
  const wsRef = useRef<WebSocket | null>(null)
  const attemptsRef = useRef(0)
  const store = useGameStore()

  const handleMessage = useCallback(
    (msg: WSMessage) => {
      switch (msg.event) {
        case 'player_joined': {
          const p = msg.payload as Parameters<typeof store.addPlayer>[0]
          store.addPlayer(p)
          break
        }
        case 'player_left':
          store.removePlayer((msg.payload as { user_id: string }).user_id)
          break
        case 'round_started': {
          const { round, pano_id, time_limit_sec } = msg.payload as {
            round: number; pano_id: string; time_limit_sec: number
          }
          store.startRound(round, pano_id, time_limit_sec)
          break
        }
        case 'guess_broadcast':
          store.setPlayerGuessed((msg.payload as { user_id: string }).user_id)
          break
        case 'round_ended': {
          const { scores, correct } = msg.payload as {
            scores: Array<{ user_id: string; score: number; distance: number }>
            correct: { x: number; y: number; floor_id: string }
          }
          store.setRoundResults(
            scores.map((s) => ({ userId: s.user_id, score: s.score, distance: s.distance })),
            { x: correct.x, y: correct.y, floorId: correct.floor_id }
          )
          break
        }
        case 'game_ended':
          store.setStatus('game_over')
          break
      }
    },
    [store]
  )

  const connect = useCallback(() => {
    if (!roomId) return
    const wsUrl = (import.meta.env.VITE_WS_URL || `ws://${location.host}`) + `/ws/rooms/${roomId}`
    const ws = new WebSocket(wsUrl)
    wsRef.current = ws

    ws.onmessage = (e) => {
      try {
        handleMessage(JSON.parse(e.data))
      } catch { /* ignore */ }
    }

    ws.onclose = () => {
      const delay = Math.min(RECONNECT_BASE_MS * 2 ** attemptsRef.current++, RECONNECT_MAX_MS)
      setTimeout(connect, delay)
    }

    ws.onopen = () => { attemptsRef.current = 0 }
  }, [roomId, handleMessage])

  useEffect(() => {
    connect()
    return () => wsRef.current?.close()
  }, [connect])

  const send = useCallback((msg: WSMessage) => {
    if (wsRef.current?.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
      wsRef.current.send(JSON.stringify(msg))
    }
  }, [])

  return { send }
}
Write scoring.test.ts
30 lines
import { describe, it, expect } from 'vitest'

const SMAX = 5000

function calculateScore(gx: number, gy: number, ax: number, ay: number, gFloor: string, aFloor: string, k = 200): number {
  if (gFloor !== aFloor) return 0
  const d = Math.sqrt((gx - ax) ** 2 + (gy - ay) ** 2)
  return Math.round(SMAX * Math.exp(-(d / k)))
}

describe('calculateScore', () => {
  it('returns max score at distance 0', () => {
    expect(calculateScore(100, 200, 100, 200, 'f1', 'f1')).toBe(5000)
  })

  it('returns 0 on floor mismatch', () => {
    expect(calculateScore(100, 200, 100, 200, 'f1', 'f2')).toBe(0)
  })

  it('decreases with distance', () => {
    const close = calculateScore(0, 0, 10, 0, 'f', 'f')
    const far = calculateScore(0, 0, 500, 0, 'f', 'f')
    expect(close).toBeGreaterThan(far)
  })

  it('approaches 0 at large distances', () => {
    expect(calculateScore(0, 0, 100000, 0, 'f', 'f')).toBe(0)
  })
})
Write auth.spec.ts
23 lines
import { test, expect } from '@playwright/test'

const BASE = process.env.E2E_BASE_URL || 'http://localhost:5173'

test('register and login', async ({ page }) => {
  await page.goto(BASE + '/register')

  await page.fill('[name=username]', 'e2e_user_' + Date.now())
  await page.fill('[name=password]', 'e2epassword123')
  await page.click('button[type=submit]')

  // Should redirect to login or home
  await expect(page).toHaveURL(/login|home|\/$/)
})

test('login with wrong password shows error', async ({ page }) => {
  await page.goto(BASE + '/login')
  await page.fill('[name=username]', 'nonexistent_user')
  await page.fill('[name=password]', 'wrongpassword')
  await page.click('button[type=submit]')
  await expect(page.locator('[data-testid=error-message]')).toBeVisible()
})

name: Tests

on:
  pull_request:
  push:
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  test-game:
    name: Go tests
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-go@v5
        with:
          go-version: "1.22"
          cache-dependency-path: services/game/go.sum
      - name: Run tests
        working-directory: services/game
        run: go test ./... -race -coverprofile=coverage.out
      - name: Check coverage >= 80%
        working-directory: services/game
        run: |
          total=$(go tool cover -func=coverage.out | grep total | awk '{print $3}' | tr -d '%')
          echo "Coverage: ${total}%"
          awk -v t="$total" 'BEGIN{if(t+0<80){print "Coverage below 80%: "t"%"; exit 1}}'

  test-workers:
    name: Python tests
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-python@v5
        with:
          python-version: "3.11"
      - name: Install system deps
        run: sudo apt-get install -y libvips-dev
      - name: Install deps
        working-directory: services/workers
        run: pip install -r requirements.txt
      - name: Run tests
        working-directory: services/workers
        run: pytest --cov=app --cov-fail-under=75 -v

  test-frontend:
    name: Frontend tests
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: 20
          cache: npm
          cache-dependency-path: frontend/package-lock.json
      - name: Install deps
        working-directory: frontend
        run: npm ci
      - name: Run tests
        working-directory: frontend
        run: npm run test -- --run --coverage

  test-admin:
    name: Admin tests
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: 20
          cache: npm
          cache-dependency-path: admin/package-lock.json
      - name: Install deps
        working-directory: admin
        run: npm ci
      - name: Run tests
        working-directory: admin
        run: npm run test -- --run

  e2e:
    name: E2E (Playwright)
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: [test-game, test-workers, test-frontend]
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: 20
      - name: Install Playwright
        working-directory: frontend
        run: npm ci && npx playwright install --with-deps chromium
      - name: Start test stack
        run: docker compose -f infra/compose/docker-compose.test.yml up -d
      - name: Wait for services
        run: sleep 15
      - name: Run E2E tests
        working-directory: frontend
        run: npx playwright test
        env:
          E2E_BASE_URL: http://localhost:5173
      - name: Stop test stack
        if: always()
        run: docker compose -f infra/compose/docker-compose.test.yml down -v
Write build-game.yml
45 lines
name: Build Game Service

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]
    paths:
      - "services/game/**"
      - ".github/workflows/build-game.yml"
    tags:
      - "game/v*"

jobs:
  build:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - uses: docker/setup-qemu-action@v3

      - uses: docker/setup-buildx-action@v3

      - uses: docker/login-action@v3
        with:
          username: ${{ secrets.DOCKERHUB_USERNAME }}
          password: ${{ secrets.DOCKERHUB_TOKEN }}

      - name: Extract metadata
        id: meta
        uses: docker/metadata-action@v5
        with:
          images: ${{ secrets.DOCKERHUB_USERNAME }}/gssr-game
          tags: |
            type=raw,value=latest,enable={{is_default_branch}}
            type=sha,prefix=,format=short

      - name: Build and push (multi-arch)
        uses: docker/build-push-action@v5
        with:
          context: services/game
          platforms: linux/amd64,linux/arm/v7
          push: true
          tags: ${{ steps.meta.outputs.tags }}
          cache-from: type=gha
          cache-to: type=gha,mode=max

Write deploy-mainpc.yml
41 lines
name: Deploy to Main PC

on:
  workflow_run:
    workflows: ["Build Game Service", "Build Workers Service"]
    types: [completed]
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  deploy:
    if: ${{ github.event.workflow_run.conclusion == 'success' }}
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: Deploy via SSH
        uses: appleboy/ssh-action@v1
        with:
          host: ${{ secrets.MAINPC_SSH_HOST }}
          username: deploy
          key: ${{ secrets.MAINPC_SSH_KEY }}
          script: |
            set -e
            cd /opt/gssr

            # Pull new images
            docker compose -f docker-compose.mainpc.yml pull workers celery

            # Restart updated services (zero-downtime for nginx/db)
            docker compose -f docker-compose.mainpc.yml up -d --no-build workers celery

            # Run migrations
            docker run --rm \
              --network gssr_default \
              -e GOOSE_DRIVER=postgres \
              -e GOOSE_DBSTRING="${DATABASE_URL}" \
              -v /opt/gssr/migrations:/migrations \
              ghcr.io/pressly/goose:latest up

            echo "Deploy complete"
        env:
          DATABASE_URL: ${{ secrets.DATABASE_URL }}
Write deploy-zynq.yml
71 lines
name: Deploy to Zynq Nodes

on:
  workflow_run:
    workflows: ["Build Game Service"]
    types: [completed]
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  deploy:
    if: ${{ github.event.workflow_run.conclusion == 'success' }}
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    strategy:
      fail-fast: false
      matrix:
        node:
          - host: ${{ secrets.ZYNQ1_HOST }}
          - host: ${{ secrets.ZYNQ2_HOST }}
          - host: ${{ secrets.ZYNQ3_HOST }}
          - host: ${{ secrets.ZYNQ4_HOST }}
          - host: ${{ secrets.ZYNQ5_HOST }}
    steps:
      - name: Deploy via Docker (preferred)
        uses: appleboy/ssh-action@v1
        with:
          host: ${{ matrix.node.host }}
          username: deploy
          key: ${{ secrets.ZYNQ_SSH_KEY }}
          script: |
            set -e
            cd /opt/gssr
            docker compose -f docker-compose.zynq.yml pull game
            docker compose -f docker-compose.zynq.yml up -d --no-build game
            echo "Zynq deploy complete"
        continue-on-error: true
        id: docker_deploy

      # Bare binary fallback (if Docker failed or not available)
      - name: Build ARM binary
        if: steps.docker_deploy.outcome == 'failure'
        uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - name: Setup Go for binary build
        if: steps.docker_deploy.outcome == 'failure'
        uses: actions/setup-go@v5
        with:
          go-version: "1.22"
      - name: Build ARM binary
        if: steps.docker_deploy.outcome == 'failure'
        working-directory: services/game
        run: make build-arm
      - name: Deploy bare binary
        if: steps.docker_deploy.outcome == 'failure'
        uses: appleboy/scp-action@v0.1.7
        with:
          host: ${{ matrix.node.host }}
          username: deploy
          key: ${{ secrets.ZYNQ_SSH_KEY }}
          source: "services/game/dist/game-server-arm"
          target: "/opt/gssr/"
      - name: Restart systemd service
        if: steps.docker_deploy.outcome == 'failure'
        uses: appleboy/ssh-action@v1
        with:
          host: ${{ matrix.node.host }}
          username: deploy
          key: ${{ secrets.ZYNQ_SSH_KEY }}
          script: |
            mv /opt/gssr/services/game/dist/game-server-arm /opt/gssr/game-server
            chmod +x /opt/gssr/game-server
            sudo systemctl restart gssr-game
Write deploy-k3s.yml
35 lines
name: Deploy to k3s (Optional)

on:
  workflow_dispatch:
    inputs:
      image_tag:
        description: "Image tag to deploy (e.g. sha-abc1234)"
        required: true
        default: "latest"

jobs:
  deploy:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: Install kubectl
        uses: azure/setup-kubectl@v4

      - name: Write kubeconfig
        run: |
          mkdir -p ~/.kube
          echo "${{ secrets.K3S_KUBECONFIG }}" > ~/.kube/config
          chmod 600 ~/.kube/config

      - name: Update image tag
        run: |
          kubectl set image deployment/game \
            game=${{ secrets.DOCKERHUB_USERNAME }}/gssr-game:${{ inputs.image_tag }} \
            -n gssr

      - name: Wait for rollout
        run: kubectl rollout status deployment/game -n gssr --timeout=120s

      - name: Verify pods
        run: kubectl get pods -n gssr -o wide

Key facts to add/update:

## Project: GSSR (GeoGuessr School Edition)
- **Type**: Self-hosted multiplayer panorama guessing game, greenfield
- **Monorepo layout**: services/game (Go Fiber), services/workers (Python FastAPI+Celery), frontend/ (React+Vite), admin/ (React+Vite), infra/ (Docker Compose + Nginx + monitoring), migrations/ (goose SQL), .github/workflows/
- **Go service**: Fiber v2, pgx/v5, go-redis/v9, golang-jwt/v5, fiberprometheus; target GOARCH=arm/v7 for Zynq nodes; Dockerfile in services/game/
- **Python workers**: FastAPI, Celery (RabbitMQ broker, Valkey backend), pyvips (tiling), onnxruntime (NSFW), minio; Dockerfile in services/workers/
- **Frontend**: React 18 + Vite + Zustand + Leaflet L.CRS.Simple + Marzipano + nsfwjs + LiveKit
- **Admin panel**: separate React+Vite app, port 5174, proxies to workers:8000
- **Infra**: Main PC runs postgres, valkey, rabbitmq, minio, livekit, nginx, cloudflared, portainer, prometheus, grafana, loki, promtail, cadvisor, node-exporter; Zynq nodes run only gssr-game container
- **Network**: Cloudflare Tunnel (cloudflared) — no open router ports. Cloudflare Access protects admin/s3/grafana/mq/portainer
- **CI/CD**: GitHub Actions → DockerHub; multi-arch build (linux/amd64 + linux/arm/v7) for game service; Cloudflare Pages for frontends
- **k3s**: Optional — k3s server on Main PC, k3s agents on Zynq nodes; manifests in infra/k8s/
- **Docs**: docs/steps/01-12-*.md — operational runbooks for each implementation step
- **Migrations**: goose SQL, 6 files: users, maps, floors, panoramas, matches, guesses
- **Scoring**: Score = 5000 * exp(-(d/K)), floor mismatch → 0
- **ELO**: K=32 for <30 matches, K=16 for ≥30; pairwise ELO recalculated by Celery task after match end
Всё готово. Вот что создано:

The user wants a local testing flow. Let me think about what this means in context of the GSSR project.

They likely want:

A docker-compose.test.yml for spinning up local test environment
A script or Makefile target to run all tests locally
Maybe a docker-compose.dev.yml for local development
Let me check what already exists and what's missing. The test.yml CI workflow references infra/compose/docker-compose.test.yml but I don't think I created it. Let me check.

I need to create:

infra/compose/docker-compose.test.yml - test environment with isolated DB

A root Makefile with convenient targets for running unit tests, integration tests, E2E tests, and local development

Possibly a docker-compose.dev.yml for the full local development stack

The distinction here is important: unit tests can run directly without Docker, but integration and E2E tests need real services like Postgres and Valkey, so I'll need docker-compose for those. The main missing piece is the test compose file and the Makefile to orchestrate everything.

Now I'll set up the Makefile with all the test targets and add a Playwright config for the frontend E2E tests.

Write docker-compose.test.yml
123 lines
name: gssr-test

# Isolated test environment — ephemeral DB/cache, no Nginx, no Cloudflare.
# Usage: docker compose -f infra/compose/docker-compose.test.yml up -d
#        <run tests>
#        docker compose -f infra/compose/docker-compose.test.yml down -v

services:
  postgres-test:
    image: postgres:16-alpine
    environment:
      POSTGRES_USER: gssr_test
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: gssr_test
      POSTGRES_DB: gssr_test
    ports:
      - "5433:5432"    # offset to avoid conflict with dev postgres on 5432
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U gssr_test -d gssr_test"]
      interval: 5s
      timeout: 3s
      retries: 10
    tmpfs:
      - /var/lib/postgresql/data   # in-memory — fast, no leftover state

  valkey-test:
    image: valkey/valkey:7-alpine
    ports:
      - "6380:6379"    # offset to avoid conflict with dev valkey

  rabbitmq-test:
    image: rabbitmq:3.13-alpine
    ports:
      - "5673:5672"    # offset

  minio-test:
    image: minio/minio:latest
    command: server /data
    environment:
      MINIO_ROOT_USER: gssr_test
      MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD: gssr_test
    ports:
      - "9002:9000"
    tmpfs:
      - /data

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - **Go Fiber v2** — game engine service on Zynq ARM v7 nodes (user chose Fiber over Gin/Echo)
   - **Python FastAPI + Celery** — worker service on Main PC (panorama tiling, NSFW moderation, ELO recalculation)
   - **pyvips / libvips** — DeepZoom tile generation for 8K panoramas
   - **onnxruntime** — NSFW model inference (nsfw.onnx, ~50MB)
   - **React + Vite + Zustand + Leaflet L.CRS.Simple + Marzipano + nsfwjs + LiveKit** — game frontend
   - **goose** — SQL migration tool (no ORM lock-in)
   - **Valkey** (Redis-compatible) — session store, Celery backend, room state
   - **RabbitMQ** — Celery broker, match-ended events
   - **MinIO S3** — tile storage, floor images, avatars
   - **LiveKit** — SFU for voice chat (server on Main PC, token generated by Go service)
   - **Cloudflare Tunnel (cloudflared)** — Zero Trust, no open router ports
   - **Cloudflare Access** — OTP-based protection for admin/s3/grafana/mq/portainer
   - **Cloudflare Pages** — frontend + admin panel static hosting
   - **Prometheus + Grafana + Loki + Promtail + cAdvisor + node-exporter** — full observability stack
   - **Portainer** — Docker management UI, exposed via Cloudflare Access
   - **k3s** — optional lightweight Kubernetes on Zynq ARM nodes (k3s server on Main PC)
   - **Multi-arch Docker builds** — `linux/amd64` + `linux/arm/v7` via QEMU in GitHub Actions
   - **Scoring formula**: `Score = 5000 * exp(-(d/K))`, floor mismatch → 0
   - **ELO**: K=32 for <30 matches, K=16 for ≥30; recalculated by Celery post-match
   - **testcontainers-go** — integration tests with real Postgres/Valkey
   - **moto** — S3 mock for Python tests
   - **Playwright** — E2E tests against docker-compose.test.yml stack
   - **JWT HttpOnly cookies** — `access_token` (15min) + `refresh_token` (7d), stored in Valkey

     ```go
     func CalculateScore(gx, gy, ax, ay float64, gFloorID, aFloorID string, k float64) int {
         if gFloorID != aFloorID { return 0 }
         d := math.Sqrt(math.Pow(gx-ax, 2) + math.Pow(gy-ay, 2))
         return int(math.Round(ScoreMax * math.Exp(-(d / k))))
     }
     ```

5. Problem Solving:
   - **Stateless Zynq nodes**: All 5 nodes share JWT_SECRET and read/write room state via Valkey on Main PC — solved the multi-node consistency problem without sticky sessions.
   - **ARM deployment flexibility**: Both Docker (arm/v7 image) and bare binary (CGO_ENABLED=0 GOOS=linux GOARCH=arm GOARM=7) supported; CI tries Docker first, falls back to binary.
   - **External access without open ports**: Cloudflare Tunnel handles all ingress; Cloudflare Access adds OTP/SSO for internal services.
   - **Large file uploads**: `client_max_body_size 100m` in Nginx for 8K panorama uploads.
   - **Test isolation**: `docker-compose.test.yml` uses `tmpfs` for postgres and minio (no leftover state), offset ports to avoid dev conflicts.

# GSSR — root Makefile
# Convenience targets for local development and testing
# Requires: docker, docker compose, go 1.22+, python 3.11+, node 20+

COMPOSE_TEST := docker compose -f infra/compose/docker-compose.test.yml
COMPOSE_DEV  := docker compose -f infra/compose/docker-compose.mainpc.yml

.PHONY: help dev dev-down test test-go test-python test-frontend e2e \
        test-up test-down lint lint-go lint-python migrate-up migrate-reset

# ─────────────────────────────────────────────
# Help
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────
help:
	@echo ""
	@echo "GSSR local targets:"
	@echo ""
	@echo "  Development"
	@echo "    make dev          — start full dev stack (Main PC services)"
	@echo "    make dev-down     — stop dev stack"
	@echo ""
	@echo "  Testing"
	@echo "    make test         — run ALL tests (Go + Python + Vitest + Playwright)"
	@echo "    make test-go      — run Go unit + integration tests"
	@echo "    make test-python  — run Python unit tests (pytest)"
	@echo "    make test-frontend— run Vitest unit tests"
	@echo "    make e2e          — start test stack + Playwright + teardown"
	@echo ""
	@echo "  Test infrastructure"
	@echo "    make test-up      — start isolated test docker-compose stack"
	@echo "    make test-down    — stop and remove test stack volumes"
	@echo ""
	@echo "  Database"
	@echo "    make migrate-up   — run goose migrations against dev postgres"
	@echo "    make migrate-reset— rollback all dev migrations (destructive)"
	@echo ""
	@echo "  Linting"
	@echo "    make lint         — run all linters"
	@echo "    make lint-go      — golangci-lint on services/game"
	@echo "    make lint-python  — ruff + mypy on services/workers"

# ─────────────────────────────────────────────
# Development stack
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────
dev:
	$(COMPOSE_DEV) up -d
	@echo "Dev stack is up. API → http://localhost:80"

dev-down:
	$(COMPOSE_DEV) down

# ─────────────────────────────────────────────
# Test infrastructure
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────
test-up:
	$(COMPOSE_TEST) up -d --build
	@echo "Waiting for test services to become healthy..."
	$(COMPOSE_TEST) wait migrate
	@echo "Test stack ready."

test-down:
	$(COMPOSE_TEST) down -v

# ─────────────────────────────────────────────
# Unit / integration tests (no docker needed)
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────
test-go:
	@echo "==> Go tests"
	cd services/game && go test ./... -race -count=1 -timeout=120s

test-python:
	@echo "==> Python tests"
	cd services/workers && python -m pytest tests/ -v --tb=short

test-frontend:
	@echo "==> Vitest"

import { defineConfig, devices } from "@playwright/test";

/**
 * E2E tests run against the isolated docker-compose test stack.
 * Start it first:  make test-up
 * Then run E2E:    npx playwright test
 * Or both at once: make e2e
 */

const GAME_URL = process.env.PLAYWRIGHT_BASE_URL ?? "http://localhost:3001";

export default defineConfig({
  testDir: "./e2e",
  fullyParallel: false, // avoid race conditions on shared test DB
  forbidOnly: !!process.env.CI,
  retries: process.env.CI ? 1 : 0,
  workers: process.env.CI ? 1 : undefined,
  reporter: process.env.CI ? "github" : "list",

  use: {
    baseURL: GAME_URL,
    trace: "on-first-retry",
    screenshot: "only-on-failure",
  },

  projects: [
    {
      name: "chromium",
      use: { ...devices["Desktop Chrome"] },
    },
  ],

  // Global setup: wait for game service healthcheck to pass
  globalSetup: "./e2e/global-setup.ts",
});

41 lines
import { request } from "@playwright/test";

const GAME_HEALTH = process.env.GAME_HEALTH_URL ?? "http://localhost:3001/health";
const WORKERS_HEALTH =
  process.env.WORKERS_HEALTH_URL ?? "http://localhost:8001/health";

const TIMEOUT_MS = 60_000;
const INTERVAL_MS = 2_000;

async function waitForService(name: string, url: string): Promise<void> {
  const deadline = Date.now() + TIMEOUT_MS;
  const ctx = await request.newContext();

  while (Date.now() < deadline) {
    try {
      const res = await ctx.get(url);
      if (res.ok()) {
        console.log(`[global-setup] ${name} is healthy`);
        await ctx.dispose();
        return;
      }
    } catch {
      // not up yet
    }
    await new Promise((r) => setTimeout(r, INTERVAL_MS));
  }

  await ctx.dispose();
  throw new Error(
    `[global-setup] Timed out waiting for ${name} at ${url}. ` +
      "Did you run 'make test-up'?"
  );
}

export default async function globalSetup(): Promise<void> {
  await Promise.all([
    waitForService("game-test", GAME_HEALTH),
    waitForService("workers-test", WORKERS_HEALTH),
  ]);
}

import { test, expect, request } from "@playwright/test";

// Game API base (test stack: game-test on port 3001)
const API = process.env.PLAYWRIGHT_API_URL ?? "http://localhost:3001";

// These tests hit the API directly (no browser UI yet — UI tests come after frontend is built)
test.describe("Auth API", () => {
  test("register + login flow", async () => {
    const ctx = await request.newContext({ baseURL: API });
    const username = `e2e_${Date.now()}`;
    const password = "e2ePassword123!";

    // Register
    const reg = await ctx.post("/api/auth/register", {
      data: { username, password },
    });
    expect(reg.status()).toBe(201);

    // Login
    const login = await ctx.post("/api/auth/login", {
      data: { username, password },
    });
    expect(login.status()).toBe(200);
    const body = await login.json();
    expect(body).toHaveProperty("user_id");

    await ctx.dispose();
  });

  test("login with wrong password returns 401", async () => {
    const ctx = await request.newContext({ baseURL: API });

    const res = await ctx.post("/api/auth/login", {
      data: { username: "nonexistent_user", password: "wrongpassword" },
    });
    expect(res.status()).toBe(401);

    await ctx.dispose();
  });

  test("access protected endpoint without token returns 401", async () => {
    const ctx = await request.newContext({ baseURL: API });

    const res = await ctx.get("/api/users/me");
    expect(res.status()).toBe(401);

    await ctx.dispose();
  });
});
Now add a game E2E spec:

Write c:\Users\catsi\Documents\GitHub\gssr\frontend\e2e\game.spec.ts
82 lines
import { test, expect, request, APIRequestContext } from "@playwright/test";

const GAME_API = process.env.PLAYWRIGHT_API_URL ?? "http://localhost:3001";

async function registerAndLogin(
  ctx: APIRequestContext,
  suffix: string
): Promise<{ userId: string }> {
  const username = `e2e_${suffix}_${Date.now()}`;
  const password = "e2ePassword123!";

  await ctx.post("/api/auth/register", { data: { username, password } });
  const login = await ctx.post("/api/auth/login", {
    data: { username, password },
  });
  const body = await login.json();
  return { userId: body.user_id };
}

test.describe("Game flow", () => {
  test("create room → join → start → guess → results", async () => {
    // Host context
    const host = await request.newContext({ baseURL: GAME_API });
    await registerAndLogin(host, "host");

    // Verify /api/users/me works after login (cookie set)
    const me = await host.get("/api/users/me");
    expect(me.status()).toBe(200);
    const meBody = await me.json();
    expect(meBody).toHaveProperty("username");

    // Get a map to play on
    const maps = await host.get("/api/maps");
    expect(maps.status()).toBe(200);
    const mapsBody = await maps.json();

    // Skip room creation if no maps exist in test DB (seed needed)
    if (!mapsBody || mapsBody.length === 0) {
      console.log("No maps in test DB — skipping room flow. Seed maps first.");
      await host.dispose();
      return;
    }

    const mapId = mapsBody[0].id;

    // Create room
    const create = await host.post("/api/rooms", {
      data: { map_id: mapId, max_players: 2, rounds: 1, time_limit_sec: 30 },
    });
    expect(create.status()).toBe(201);
    const room = await create.json();
    expect(room).toHaveProperty("id");
    const roomId = room.id;

    // Second player joins
    const player = await request.newContext({ baseURL: GAME_API });
    await registerAndLogin(player, "player");
    const join = await player.post(`/api/rooms/${roomId}/join`);
    expect(join.status()).toBe(200);

    // Host starts game
    const start = await host.post(`/api/rooms/${roomId}/start`);
    expect(start.status()).toBe(200);

    // Fetch room state — should have a current pano
    const state = await host.get(`/api/rooms/${roomId}`);
    expect(state.status()).toBe(200);
    const stateBody = await state.json();
    expect(stateBody.status).toBe("active");

    await host.dispose();
    await player.dispose();
  });

  test("GET /health returns 200", async () => {
    const ctx = await request.newContext({ baseURL: GAME_API });
    const res = await ctx.get("/health");
    expect(res.status()).toBe(200);
    await ctx.dispose();
  });
});

# GitHub Actions — Secrets & Variables reference

#   Repository → Settings → Secrets and variables → Actions
#
# SECRETS  (encrypted, never shown in logs)  → "New repository secret"
# VARIABLES (plain text, visible in logs)    → "New repository variable"
# ============================================================

# SECRETS
# ────────────────────────────────────────────

# --- DockerHub (build-game.yml, build-workers.yml, deploy-k3s.yml) ---
DOCKERHUB_USERNAME=your-dockerhub-username

# Generate at: https://hub.docker.com/settings/security → New Access Token

# --- Cloudflare (deploy-frontend.yml, deploy-admin.yml) ---

# Generate at: Cloudflare Dashboard → My Profile → API Tokens
# Required permission: "Cloudflare Pages: Edit" for your account

# Found at: Cloudflare Dashboard → right sidebar on any domain

# --- Main PC SSH (deploy-mainpc.yml) ---
MAINPC_SSH_HOST=192.168.1.100
# IP or hostname of your main PC (must be reachable from GitHub runners via Cloudflare Tunnel or public IP)
MAINPC_SSH_KEY=-----BEGIN OPENSSH PRIVATE KEY-----
# Full private key content (RSA or Ed25519).
# Generate: ssh-keygen -t ed25519 -C "github-actions-deploy"
# Add public key to /home/deploy/.ssh/authorized_keys on Main PC

# --- Main PC database URL (deploy-mainpc.yml — goose migrations) ---
DATABASE_URL=postgres://gssr:STRONGPASSWORD@localhost:5432/gssr?sslmode=disable

# Full kubeconfig YAML content (base64 or raw).
# Get from Main PC: sudo cat /etc/rancher/k3s/k3s.yaml

ci/cd требует настройки чего-то кроме github secrets?
The user is asking whether the CI/CD requires setting up anything beyond GitHub secrets. Let me think about this carefully by reviewing the workflows and what they depend on.

Let me check the workflows to understand all external dependencies.

Read c:\Users\catsi\Documents\GitHub\gssr\.github\workflows\build-game.yml

Нет, кроме GitHub Secrets нужно ещё несколько вещей. Вот полный чеклист:

Что нужно настроить помимо GitHub Secrets
1. DockerHub — создать репозитории
На hub.docker.com вручную создать два публичных (или приватных) репозитория:


<DOCKERHUB_USERNAME>/gssr-game
<DOCKERHUB_USERNAME>/gssr-workers
Без этого docker/build-push-action упадёт с 404.

2. Cloudflare Pages — создать два проекта
В Cloudflare Dashboard → Pages → Create application → Direct Upload (не Connect to Git):


gssr-frontend   ← используется в deploy-frontend.yml
gssr-admin      ← используется в deploy-admin.yml
Имена проектов должны совпадать с --project-name= в workflows. Первый деплой через wrangler создаёт проект автоматически, но только если API Token имеет права Cloudflare Pages: Edit на уровне аккаунта, а не зоны.

3. Main PC — подготовить deploy пользователя

# На Main PC
sudo useradd -m -s /bin/bash deploy
sudo mkdir -p /home/deploy/.ssh
sudo bash -c 'echo "PUBLIC_KEY_CONTENT" >> /home/deploy/.ssh/authorized_keys'
sudo chmod 700 /home/deploy/.ssh && sudo chmod 600 /home/deploy/.ssh/authorized_keys
sudo chown -R deploy:deploy /home/deploy/.ssh

# Папка проекта
sudo mkdir -p /opt/gssr/migrations
sudo chown -R deploy:deploy /opt/gssr

# Docker без sudo
sudo usermod -aG docker deploy
И скопировать migrations/ + infra/compose/docker-compose.mainpc.yml на Main PC в /opt/gssr/.

4. Zynq ноды — то же самое для deploy

# На каждом Zynq
sudo useradd -m -s /bin/bash deploy
# ... (тот же authorized_keys, что и ZYNQ_SSH_KEY публичная часть)
sudo mkdir -p /opt/gssr
sudo chown deploy:deploy /opt/gssr
sudo usermod -aG docker deploy

# Если используется bare binary — systemd юнит:
sudo cp gssr-game.service /etc/systemd/system/
sudo systemctl daemon-reload
# Право перезапускать без пароля:
echo 'deploy ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD: /bin/systemctl restart gssr-game' \
  | sudo tee /etc/sudoers.d/gssr-deploy
5. Main PC — SSH доступен снаружи
deploy-mainpc.yml коннектится к MAINPC_SSH_HOST с GitHub runner-а. Варианты:

Cloudflare Tunnel (cloudflared access ssh) — рекомендуется, не открывает порт наружу
Публичный IP + SSH на нестандартном порту — проще, но менее безопасно
6. k3s (если используется) — kubeconfig

# На Main PC после установки k3s
sudo cat /etc/rancher/k3s/k3s.yaml
# Заменить server: https://127.0.0.1:6443
# на server: https://<MAINPC_EXTERNAL_IP>:6443
# Вставить содержимое целиком в GitHub Secret K3S_KUBECONFIG
Итого: что нужно один раз до первого push в main
#	Действие	Где
1	Создать gssr-game и gssr-workers на DockerHub	hub.docker.com
2	Создать проекты gssr-frontend и gssr-admin на Cloudflare Pages	dash.cloudflare.com
3	Добавить deploy юзера + SSH key на Main PC	SSH на Main PC
4	Добавить deploy юзера + SSH key на каждый Zynq	SSH на каждый Zynq
5	Положить docker-compose.mainpc.yml + .env + migrations/ в /opt/gssr/ на Main PC	SCP/SSH
6	Положить docker-compose.zynq.yml + .env в /opt/gssr/ на каждый Zynq	SCP/SSH
7	Заполнить все GitHub Secrets и Variables	GitHub → Settings
8	(опц.) Настроить kubeconfig для k3s	Main PC
ci/cd flow не перемещает compose, не создаёт .env, не перемещает папки? почему?
The user is asking a good question: the CI/CD workflows (deploy-mainpc.yml, deploy-zynq.yml) assume that files like docker-compose.mainpc.yml, .env, and migrations/ are already on the server. But the workflows don't actually deploy these files - they just SSH in and run docker compose pull + docker compose up.

The user is pointing out that the CI/CD flow is incomplete - it doesn't:

Copy docker-compose.mainpc.yml / docker-compose.zynq.yml to the servers

Create/update .env files on the servers

Set up directory structures on the servers

Copy migrations/ to the servers (though the mainpc workflow runs goose via docker with a local volume mount)

This is a legitimate gap. The typical solutions would be to use scp to push the compose files and config during deployment, have the server pull directly from git, or set up a separate bootstrap workflow for initial setup while the deploy workflow just handles image updates. Let me examine what the current deploy-mainpc.yml actually does versus what it needs to do.

The mainpc deployment SSHes in, navigates to /opt/gssr, pulls and starts the workers and celery services via docker compose, then runs goose migrations with a volume mount to the migrations directory. This assumes the compose file, environment file, and migrations directory are already present on the server. The zynq deployment follows a similar pattern—SSH in, pull the game service image, and start it—but only handles a single service per device.

The real issue is that neither workflow actually gets the infrastructure files onto the servers in the first place. The CI/CD needs to check out the repo, SCP over the compose files, migrations, nginx config, and other artifacts, then handle the .env file either by having it pre-created on the server as a one-time setup or by constructing it from GitHub Secrets and copying it over during each deployment. I'm laying out the specific file transfers and commands for each deployment workflow—mainpc needs the compose file, migrations, and infrastructure configs, while zynq is simpler with just its compose file. Both will construct their respective .env files from secrets during the CI step before transferring them. I should also consider adding a separate bootstrap workflow for initial server setup since these workflows assume the infrastructure already exists. me redesign the workflows:

deploy-mainpc.yml - needs to:

Checkout
Create .env file locally from secrets
SCP: docker-compose.mainpc.yml → /opt/gssr/
SCP: migrations/ → /opt/gssr/
SCP: infra/nginx/ → /opt/gssr/nginx/ (nginx.conf)
SCP: infra/monitoring/ → /opt/gssr/monitoring/
SCP: .env → /opt/gssr/.env
SSH: mkdir -p /opt/gssr, docker compose pull, docker compose up -d, goose up
deploy-zynq.yml - needs to:

Checkout
Create .env.zynq locally
SCP: docker-compose.zynq.yml → /opt/gssr/
SCP: .env.zynq → /opt/gssr/.env
SSH: docker compose pull + up

name: Deploy to Main PC

on:
  workflow_run:
    workflows: ["Build Game Service", "Build Workers Service"]
    types: [completed]

jobs:

    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: Deploy via SSH
        uses: appleboy/ssh-action@v1
        env:
          GH_DEPLOY_TOKEN:    ${{ secrets.GH_DEPLOY_TOKEN }}
          POSTGRES_PASSWORD:  ${{ secrets.POSTGRES_PASSWORD }}
          RABBITMQ_PASS:      ${{ secrets.RABBITMQ_PASS }}
          MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD: ${{ secrets.MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD }}
          JWT_SECRET:         ${{ secrets.JWT_SECRET }}
          LIVEKIT_API_KEY:    ${{ secrets.LIVEKIT_API_KEY }}
          LIVEKIT_API_SECRET: ${{ secrets.LIVEKIT_API_SECRET }}
          GRAFANA_PASSWORD:   ${{ secrets.GRAFANA_PASSWORD }}
          DOCKERHUB_USERNAME: ${{ secrets.DOCKERHUB_USERNAME }}
          DOMAIN:             ${{ vars.DOMAIN }}
        with:
          host:     ${{ secrets.MAINPC_SSH_HOST }}
          username: deploy
          key:      ${{ secrets.MAINPC_SSH_KEY }}
          envs:     GH_DEPLOY_TOKEN,POSTGRES_PASSWORD,RABBITMQ_PASS,MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD,JWT_SECRET,LIVEKIT_API_KEY,LIVEKIT_API_SECRET,GRAFANA_PASSWORD,DOCKERHUB_USERNAME,DOMAIN
          script: |
            set -e
            cd /opt/gssr

            # ── 1. Pull latest code ──────────────────────────────────────
            git -c "url.https://${GH_DEPLOY_TOKEN}@github.com/.insteadOf=https://github.com/" \
              pull origin main

            # ── 2. Write infra/compose/.env from secrets ─────────────────
            # Using printf to safely handle special characters in values
            {
              printf 'POSTGRES_USER=gssr\n'
              printf 'POSTGRES_PASSWORD=%s\n'      "${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}"
              printf 'POSTGRES_DB=gssr\n'
              printf 'DATABASE_URL=postgres://gssr:%s@postgres:5432/gssr?sslmode=disable\n' "${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}"
              printf 'VALKEY_URL=redis://valkey:6379\n'
              printf 'RABBITMQ_USER=gssr\n'
              printf 'RABBITMQ_PASS=%s\n'          "${RABBITMQ_PASS}"
              printf 'RABBITMQ_URL=amqp://gssr:%s@rabbitmq:5672/\n' "${RABBITMQ_PASS}"
              printf 'MINIO_ROOT_USER=gssr\n'
              printf 'MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD=%s\n'    "${MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD}"
              printf 'MINIO_ENDPOINT=minio:9000\n'
              printf 'MINIO_BUCKET=gssr\n'
              printf 'POSTGRES_URL=postgres://gssr:%s@postgres:5432/gssr?sslmode=disable\n' "${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}"
              printf 'JWT_SECRET=%s\n'             "${JWT_SECRET}"
              printf 'JWT_ACCESS_TTL=15m\n'
              printf 'JWT_REFRESH_TTL=168h\n'
              printf 'WORKERS_DATABASE_URL=postgresql+asyncpg://gssr:%s@postgres:5432/gssr\n' "${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}"
              printf 'ADMIN_JWT_SECRET=%s\n'       "${JWT_SECRET}"
              printf 'CORS_ORIGINS=https://%s\n'  "${DOMAIN}"
              printf 'ADMIN_CORS_ORIGINS=https://admin.%s\n' "${DOMAIN}"
              printf 'NSFW_MODEL_PATH=/app/models/nsfw.onnx\n'
              printf 'NSFW_THRESHOLD=0.7\n'
              printf 'LIVEKIT_URL=ws://livekit:7880\n'
              printf 'LIVEKIT_API_KEY=%s\n'        "${LIVEKIT_API_KEY}"
              printf 'LIVEKIT_API_SECRET=%s\n'     "${LIVEKIT_API_SECRET}"
              printf 'GRAFANA_PASSWORD=%s\n'       "${GRAFANA_PASSWORD}"
              printf 'DOMAIN=%s\n'                 "${DOMAIN}"
              printf 'DOCKERHUB_USERNAME=%s\n'     "${DOCKERHUB_USERNAME}"
            } > infra/compose/.env

            # ── 3. Pull new images ────────────────────────────────────────
            docker compose -f infra/compose/docker-compose.mainpc.yml pull workers celery

            # ── 4. Restart updated services (db/valkey/nginx stay running) ─
            docker compose -f infra/compose/docker-compose.mainpc.yml \
              up -d --no-build workers celery

            # ── 5. Run database migrations ────────────────────────────────
            docker run --rm \
              --network gssr_default \
              -v "$(pwd)/migrations:/migrations" \
              ghcr.io/pressly/goose:latest \
              -dir /migrations postgres \
              "postgres://gssr:${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/gssr?sslmode=disable" up

            echo "Deploy complete"

They're questioning whether cloning on mainpc makes sense, suggesting we could archive and transfer via SCP instead. That's a fair point — git clone requires a GitHub token on the server which is a security risk, plus git needs to be installed. An archive approach would be simpler and avoid storing credentials.

The SCP method would work like this: during CI, create a compressed archive of the repo, transfer it to the server via SCP, then extract and deploy. This keeps all git operations on the CI side and only requires SSH access on the server.

name: Deploy to Main PC

# Triggered after either build workflow succeeds on main.
# Strategy: CI packs a git archive and SCPs it to the server.
# The server never needs git or a GitHub token.

on:
  workflow_run:
    workflows: ["Build Game Service", "Build Workers Service"]
    types: [completed]
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  deploy:
    if: ${{ github.event.workflow_run.conclusion == 'success' }}
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      # ── 1. Pack the repo into a tarball (no .git, no gitignored files) ──
      - name: Create deploy archive
        run: git archive HEAD -o deploy.tar.gz

      # ── 2. Upload archive to server ─────────────────────────────────────
      - name: Upload archive
        uses: appleboy/scp-action@v0.1.7
        with:
          host:     ${{ secrets.MAINPC_SSH_HOST }}
          username: deploy
          key:      ${{ secrets.MAINPC_SSH_KEY }}
          source:   deploy.tar.gz
          target:   /tmp/

      # ── 3. Extract + write .env + deploy ────────────────────────────────
      - name: Deploy
        uses: appleboy/ssh-action@v1
        env:
          POSTGRES_PASSWORD:   ${{ secrets.POSTGRES_PASSWORD }}
          RABBITMQ_PASS:       ${{ secrets.RABBITMQ_PASS }}
          MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD: ${{ secrets.MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD }}
          JWT_SECRET:          ${{ secrets.JWT_SECRET }}
          LIVEKIT_API_KEY:     ${{ secrets.LIVEKIT_API_KEY }}
          LIVEKIT_API_SECRET:  ${{ secrets.LIVEKIT_API_SECRET }}
          GRAFANA_PASSWORD:    ${{ secrets.GRAFANA_PASSWORD }}
          DOCKERHUB_USERNAME:  ${{ secrets.DOCKERHUB_USERNAME }}
          DOMAIN:              ${{ vars.DOMAIN }}
        with:
          host:     ${{ secrets.MAINPC_SSH_HOST }}
          username: deploy
          key:      ${{ secrets.MAINPC_SSH_KEY }}
          envs:     POSTGRES_PASSWORD,RABBITMQ_PASS,MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD,JWT_SECRET,LIVEKIT_API_KEY,LIVEKIT_API_SECRET,GRAFANA_PASSWORD,DOCKERHUB_USERNAME,DOMAIN
          script: |
            set -e
            mkdir -p /opt/gssr
            tar -xzf /tmp/deploy.tar.gz -C /opt/gssr
            rm -f /tmp/deploy.tar.gz
            cd /opt/gssr

            # Write infra/compose/.env
            # printf safely handles special characters (no heredoc expansion risks)
            {
              printf 'POSTGRES_USER=gssr\n'
              printf 'POSTGRES_PASSWORD=%s\n'      "${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}"
              printf 'POSTGRES_DB=gssr\n'
              printf 'DATABASE_URL=postgres://gssr:%s@postgres:5432/gssr?sslmode=disable\n' "${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}"
              printf 'VALKEY_URL=redis://valkey:6379\n'
              printf 'RABBITMQ_USER=gssr\n'
              printf 'RABBITMQ_PASS=%s\n'          "${RABBITMQ_PASS}"
              printf 'RABBITMQ_URL=amqp://gssr:%s@rabbitmq:5672/\n' "${RABBITMQ_PASS}"
              printf 'MINIO_ROOT_USER=gssr\n'
              printf 'MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD=%s\n'    "${MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD}"
              printf 'MINIO_ENDPOINT=minio:9000\n'
              printf 'MINIO_BUCKET=gssr\n'
              printf 'POSTGRES_URL=postgres://gssr:%s@postgres:5432/gssr?sslmode=disable\n' "${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}"
              printf 'JWT_SECRET=%s\n'             "${JWT_SECRET}"
              printf 'JWT_ACCESS_TTL=15m\n'
              printf 'JWT_REFRESH_TTL=168h\n'
              printf 'WORKERS_DATABASE_URL=postgresql+asyncpg://gssr:%s@postgres:5432/gssr\n' "${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}"
              printf 'ADMIN_JWT_SECRET=%s\n'       "${JWT_SECRET}"
              printf 'CORS_ORIGINS=https://%s\n'  "${DOMAIN}"
              printf 'ADMIN_CORS_ORIGINS=https://admin.%s\n' "${DOMAIN}"
              printf 'NSFW_MODEL_PATH=/app/models/nsfw.onnx\n'
              printf 'NSFW_THRESHOLD=0.7\n'
              printf 'LIVEKIT_URL=ws://livekit:7880\n'
              printf 'LIVEKIT_API_KEY=%s\n'        "${LIVEKIT_API_KEY}"
              printf 'LIVEKIT_API_SECRET=%s\n'     "${LIVEKIT_API_SECRET}"
              printf 'GRAFANA_PASSWORD=%s\n'       "${GRAFANA_PASSWORD}"
              printf 'DOMAIN=%s\n'                 "${DOMAIN}"
              printf 'DOCKERHUB_USERNAME=%s\n'     "${DOCKERHUB_USERNAME}"
            } > infra/compose/.env

            # Write infra/compose/livekit.yaml (contains API keys, not in git)
            cat > infra/compose/livekit.yaml <<LKEOF
            port: 7880
            rtc:
              port_range_start: 50000
              port_range_end: 60000
              tcp_port: 7881
            keys:
              ${LIVEKIT_API_KEY}: ${LIVEKIT_API_SECRET}
            logging:
              level: info
            LKEOF

            # Pull new images for workers + celery only
            # (postgres/valkey/nginx/etc keep running unchanged)
            docker compose -f infra/compose/docker-compose.mainpc.yml pull workers celery

            docker compose -f infra/compose/docker-compose.mainpc.yml \
              up -d --no-build workers celery

            # Run database migrations
            docker run --rm \
              --network gssr_default \
              -v "$(pwd)/migrations:/migrations" \
              ghcr.io/pressly/goose:latest \
              -dir /migrations postgres \
              "postgres://gssr:${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/gssr?sslmode=disable" up

            echo "Deploy complete"

name: Deploy to Main PC

on:
  workflow_run:
    workflows: ["Build Game Service", "Build Workers Service"]
    types: [completed]
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  deploy:
    if: ${{ github.event.workflow_run.conclusion == 'success' }}
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: Deploy via SSH
        uses: appleboy/ssh-action@v1
        with:
          host: ${{ secrets.MAINPC_SSH_HOST }}
          username: deploy
          key: ${{ secrets.MAINPC_SSH_KEY }}
          script: |
            set -e
            cd /opt/gssr

            # Pull new images
            docker compose -f docker-compose.mainpc.yml pull workers celery

            # Restart updated services (zero-downtime for nginx/db)
            docker compose -f docker-compose.mainpc.yml up -d --no-build workers celery

            # Run migrations
            docker run --rm \
              --network gssr_default \
              -e GOOSE_DRIVER=postgres \
              -e GOOSE_DBSTRING="${DATABASE_URL}" \
              -v /opt/gssr/migrations:/migrations \
              ghcr.io/pressly/goose:latest up

            echo "Deploy complete"
        env:
          DATABASE_URL: ${{ secrets.DATABASE_URL }}
Bash Read both files for overwrite

name: Deploy to Zynq Nodes

on:
  workflow_run:
    workflows: ["Build Game Service"]
    types: [completed]
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  deploy:
    if: ${{ github.event.workflow_run.conclusion == 'success' }}
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    strategy:
      fail-fast: false
      matrix:
        node:
          - host: ${{ secrets.ZYNQ1_HOST }}
          - host: ${{ secrets.ZYNQ2_HOST }}
          - host: ${{ secrets.ZYNQ3_HOST }}
          - host: ${{ secrets.ZYNQ4_HOST }}
          - host: ${{ secrets.ZYNQ5_HOST }}
    steps:
      - name: Deploy via Docker (preferred)
        uses: appleboy/ssh-action@v1
        with:
          host: ${{ matrix.node.host }}
          username: deploy
          key: ${{ secrets.ZYNQ_SSH_KEY }}
          script: |
            set -e
            cd /opt/gssr
            docker compose -f docker-compose.zynq.yml pull game
            docker compose -f docker-compose.zynq.yml up -d --no-build game
            echo "Zynq deploy complete"
        continue-on-error: true
        id: docker_deploy

      # Bare binary fallback (if Docker failed or not available)
      - name: Build ARM binary
        if: steps.docker_deploy.outcome == 'failure'
        uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - name: Setup Go for binary build
        if: steps.docker_deploy.outcome == 'failure'
        uses: actions/setup-go@v5
        with:
          go-version: "1.22"
      - name: Build ARM binary
        if: steps.docker_deploy.outcome == 'failure'
        working-directory: services/game
        run: make build-arm
      - name: Deploy bare binary
        if: steps.docker_deploy.outcome == 'failure'
        uses: appleboy/scp-action@v0.1.7
        with:
          host: ${{ matrix.node.host }}
          username: deploy
          key: ${{ secrets.ZYNQ_SSH_KEY }}
          source: "services/game/dist/game-server-arm"
          target: "/opt/gssr/"
      - name: Restart systemd service
        if: steps.docker_deploy.outcome == 'failure'
        uses: appleboy/ssh-action@v1
        with:
          host: ${{ matrix.node.host }}
          username: deploy
          key: ${{ secrets.ZYNQ_SSH_KEY }}
          script: |
            mv /opt/gssr/services/game/dist/game-server-arm /opt/gssr/game-server
            chmod +x /opt/gssr/game-server
            sudo systemctl restart gssr-game
name: Tests

on:
  pull_request:
  push:
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  test-game:
    name: Go tests
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-go@v5
        with:
          go-version: "1.22"
          cache-dependency-path: services/game/go.sum
      - name: Run tests
        working-directory: services/game
        run: go test ./... -race -coverprofile=coverage.out
      - name: Check coverage >= 80%
        working-directory: services/game
        run: |
          total=$(go tool cover -func=coverage.out | grep total | awk '{print $3}' | tr -d '%')
          echo "Coverage: ${total}%"
          awk -v t="$total" 'BEGIN{if(t+0<80){print "Coverage below 80%: "t"%"; exit 1}}'

  test-workers:
    name: Python tests
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-python@v5
        with:
          python-version: "3.11"
      - name: Install system deps
        run: sudo apt-get install -y libvips-dev
      - name: Install deps
        working-directory: services/workers
        run: pip install -r requirements.txt
      - name: Run tests
        working-directory: services/workers
        run: pytest --cov=app --cov-fail-under=75 -v

  test-frontend:
    name: Frontend tests
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: 20
          cache: npm
          cache-dependency-path: frontend/package-lock.json
      - name: Install deps
        working-directory: frontend
        run: npm ci
      - name: Run tests
        working-directory: frontend
        run: npm run test -- --run --coverage

  test-admin:
    name: Admin tests
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: 20
          cache: npm
          cache-dependency-path: admin/package-lock.json
      - name: Install deps
        working-directory: admin
        run: npm ci
      - name: Run tests
        working-directory: admin
        run: npm run test -- --run

  e2e:
    name: E2E (Playwright)
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: [test-game, test-workers, test-frontend]
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: 20
      - name: Install Playwright
        working-directory: frontend
        run: npm ci && npx playwright install --with-deps chromium
      - name: Start test stack
        run: docker compose -f infra/compose/docker-compose.test.yml up -d
      - name: Wait for services
        run: sleep 15
      - name: Run E2E tests
        working-directory: frontend
        run: npx playwright test
        env:
          E2E_BASE_URL: http://localhost:5173
      - name: Stop test stack
        if: always()
        run: docker compose -f infra/compose/docker-compose.test.yml down -v

# Triggered after either build workflow succeeds on main.

on:

            # Write infra/compose/.env from secrets passed as env vars.
            # printf handles special characters safely (no heredoc expansion issues).
            {
              printf 'POSTGRES_USER=gssr\n'
              printf 'POSTGRES_PASSWORD=%s\n'      "${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}"
              printf 'POSTGRES_DB=gssr\n'

              printf 'ADMIN_JWT_SECRET=%s\n'       "${JWT_SECRET}"
              printf 'CORS_ORIGINS=https://%s\n'  "${DOMAIN}"
              printf 'ADMIN_CORS_ORIGINS=https://admin.%s\n' "${DOMAIN}"

              printf 'DOMAIN=%s\n'                 "${DOMAIN}"
              printf 'DOCKERHUB_USERNAME=%s\n'     "${DOCKERHUB_USERNAME}"
            } > infra/compose/.env

            # Write livekit.yaml (contains API keys — not stored in git)
            printf 'port: 7880\nrtc:\n  port_range_start: 50000\n  port_range_end: 60000\n  tcp_port: 7881\nkeys:\n  %s: %s\nlogging:\n  level: info\n' \
              "${LIVEKIT_API_KEY}" "${LIVEKIT_API_SECRET}" \
              > infra/compose/livekit.yaml

            # Pull new images for workers + celery only
            docker compose -f infra/compose/docker-compose.mainpc.yml pull workers celery

            docker compose -f infra/compose/docker-compose.mainpc.yml \
              up -d --no-build workers celery

            # Run database migrations
            docker run --rm \
              --network gssr_default \
              -v "$(pwd)/migrations:/migrations" \
              ghcr.io/pressly/goose:latest \
              -dir /migrations postgres \
              "postgres://gssr:${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/gssr?sslmode=disable" up

            echo "Deploy complete"

name: Deploy to Zynq Nodes

# Triggered after game service build succeeds on main.
# Strategy: SCP the compose file, then SSH to write .env and restart the container.
# Bare binary fallback if Docker is unavailable on a node.

on:
  workflow_run:
    workflows: ["Build Game Service"]
    types: [completed]
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  deploy:
    if: ${{ github.event.workflow_run.conclusion == 'success' }}
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    strategy:
      fail-fast: false
      matrix:
        node:
          - host: ${{ secrets.ZYNQ1_HOST }}
          - host: ${{ secrets.ZYNQ2_HOST }}
          - host: ${{ secrets.ZYNQ3_HOST }}
          - host: ${{ secrets.ZYNQ4_HOST }}
          - host: ${{ secrets.ZYNQ5_HOST }}
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      # ── 1. Copy compose file to Zynq ─────────────────────────────────────
      - name: Upload compose file
        uses: appleboy/scp-action@v0.1.7
        with:
          host:             ${{ matrix.node.host }}
          username:         deploy
          key:              ${{ secrets.ZYNQ_SSH_KEY }}
          source:           infra/compose/docker-compose.zynq.yml
          target:           /opt/gssr/
          strip_components: 2   # strips infra/compose/ → file lands at /opt/gssr/docker-compose.zynq.yml

      # ── 2. Write .env + pull + restart (Docker preferred) ────────────────
      - name: Deploy via Docker
        id: docker_deploy
        continue-on-error: true
        uses: appleboy/ssh-action@v1
        env:
          DOCKERHUB_USERNAME: ${{ secrets.DOCKERHUB_USERNAME }}
          JWT_SECRET:         ${{ secrets.JWT_SECRET }}
          LIVEKIT_API_KEY:    ${{ secrets.LIVEKIT_API_KEY }}
          LIVEKIT_API_SECRET: ${{ secrets.LIVEKIT_API_SECRET }}
          ZYNQ_POSTGRES_URL:  ${{ secrets.ZYNQ_POSTGRES_URL }}
          ZYNQ_VALKEY_URL:    ${{ secrets.ZYNQ_VALKEY_URL }}
          DOMAIN:             ${{ vars.DOMAIN }}
        with:
          host:     ${{ matrix.node.host }}
          username: deploy
          key:      ${{ secrets.ZYNQ_SSH_KEY }}
          envs:     DOCKERHUB_USERNAME,JWT_SECRET,LIVEKIT_API_KEY,LIVEKIT_API_SECRET,ZYNQ_POSTGRES_URL,ZYNQ_VALKEY_URL,DOMAIN
          script: |
            set -e
            mkdir -p /opt/gssr
            cd /opt/gssr

            # Write .env (game service reads env_file: .env relative to compose file)
            {
              printf 'DOCKERHUB_USERNAME=%s\n'  "${DOCKERHUB_USERNAME}"
              printf 'PORT=3000\n'
              printf 'METRICS_PORT=2112\n'
              printf 'POSTGRES_URL=%s\n'        "${ZYNQ_POSTGRES_URL}"
              printf 'VALKEY_URL=%s\n'          "${ZYNQ_VALKEY_URL}"
              printf 'JWT_SECRET=%s\n'          "${JWT_SECRET}"
              printf 'JWT_ACCESS_TTL=15m\n'
              printf 'JWT_REFRESH_TTL=168h\n'
              printf 'LIVEKIT_URL=ws://livekit:7880\n'
              printf 'LIVEKIT_API_KEY=%s\n'     "${LIVEKIT_API_KEY}"
              printf 'LIVEKIT_API_SECRET=%s\n'  "${LIVEKIT_API_SECRET}"
              printf 'CORS_ORIGINS=https://%s\n' "${DOMAIN}"
            } > .env

            docker compose -f docker-compose.zynq.yml pull game
            docker compose -f docker-compose.zynq.yml up -d --no-build game
            echo "Zynq Docker deploy complete"

      # ── Bare binary fallback (if Docker unavailable on this node) ─────────
      - name: Build ARM binary
        if: steps.docker_deploy.outcome == 'failure'
        uses: actions/setup-go@v5
        with:
          go-version: "1.22"

      - name: Compile ARM binary
        if: steps.docker_deploy.outcome == 'failure'
        working-directory: services/game
        run: make build-arm

      - name: Upload binary
        if: steps.docker_deploy.outcome == 'failure'
        uses: appleboy/scp-action@v0.1.7
        with:
          host:     ${{ matrix.node.host }}
          username: deploy
          key:      ${{ secrets.ZYNQ_SSH_KEY }}
          source:   services/game/dist/game-server-arm
          target:   /opt/gssr/
          strip_components: 3   # strips services/game/dist/

      - name: Write .env + restart systemd
        if: steps.docker_deploy.outcome == 'failure'
        uses: appleboy/ssh-action@v1
        env:
          JWT_SECRET:         ${{ secrets.JWT_SECRET }}
          LIVEKIT_API_KEY:    ${{ secrets.LIVEKIT_API_KEY }}
          LIVEKIT_API_SECRET: ${{ secrets.LIVEKIT_API_SECRET }}
          ZYNQ_POSTGRES_URL:  ${{ secrets.ZYNQ_POSTGRES_URL }}
          ZYNQ_VALKEY_URL:    ${{ secrets.ZYNQ_VALKEY_URL }}
          DOMAIN:             ${{ vars.DOMAIN }}
        with:
          host:     ${{ matrix.node.host }}
          username: deploy
          key:      ${{ secrets.ZYNQ_SSH_KEY }}
          envs:     JWT_SECRET,LIVEKIT_API_KEY,LIVEKIT_API_SECRET,ZYNQ_POSTGRES_URL,ZYNQ_VALKEY_URL,DOMAIN
          script: |
            set -e
            cd /opt/gssr
            chmod +x game-server-arm
            mv game-server-arm game-server

            # Write /etc/gssr-game.env for systemd EnvironmentFile=
            {
              printf 'PORT=3000\n'
              printf 'METRICS_PORT=2112\n'
              printf 'POSTGRES_URL=%s\n'        "${ZYNQ_POSTGRES_URL}"
              printf 'VALKEY_URL=%s\n'          "${ZYNQ_VALKEY_URL}"
              printf 'JWT_SECRET=%s\n'          "${JWT_SECRET}"
              printf 'JWT_ACCESS_TTL=15m\n'
              printf 'JWT_REFRESH_TTL=168h\n'
              printf 'LIVEKIT_URL=ws://livekit:7880\n'
              printf 'LIVEKIT_API_KEY=%s\n'     "${LIVEKIT_API_KEY}"
              printf 'LIVEKIT_API_SECRET=%s\n'  "${LIVEKIT_API_SECRET}"
              printf 'CORS_ORIGINS=https://%s\n' "${DOMAIN}"
            } | sudo tee /etc/gssr-game.env > /dev/null

            sudo systemctl restart gssr-game
            echo "Zynq bare binary deploy complete"

name: Tests

on:
  pull_request:
  push:
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  test-game:
    name: Go tests
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-go@v5
        with:
          go-version: "1.22"
          cache-dependency-path: services/game/go.sum
      - name: Run tests
        working-directory: services/game
        run: go test ./... -race -coverprofile=coverage.out
      - name: Check coverage >= 80%
        working-directory: services/game
        run: |
          total=$(go tool cover -func=coverage.out | grep total | awk '{print $3}' | tr -d '%')
          echo "Coverage: ${total}%"
          awk -v t="$total" 'BEGIN{if(t+0<80){print "Coverage below 80%: "t"%"; exit 1}}'

  test-workers:
    name: Python tests
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-python@v5
        with:
          python-version: "3.11"
      - name: Install system deps
        run: sudo apt-get install -y libvips-dev
      - name: Install deps
        working-directory: services/workers
        run: pip install -r requirements.txt
      - name: Run tests
        working-directory: services/workers
        run: pytest --cov=app --cov-fail-under=75 -v

  test-frontend:
    name: Frontend tests
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: 20
          cache: npm
          cache-dependency-path: frontend/package-lock.json
      - name: Install deps
        working-directory: frontend
        run: npm ci
      - name: Run tests
        working-directory: frontend
        run: npm run test -- --run --coverage

  test-admin:
    name: Admin tests
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: 20
          cache: npm
          cache-dependency-path: admin/package-lock.json
      - name: Install deps
        working-directory: admin
        run: npm ci
      - name: Run tests
        working-directory: admin
        run: npm run test -- --run

  e2e:
    name: E2E (Playwright)
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: [test-game, test-workers, test-frontend]
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: 20

      - name: Install Playwright
        working-directory: frontend
        run: npm ci && npx playwright install --with-deps chromium

      # --build forces local image rebuild from source (no registry pull needed)
      - name: Start test stack
        run: docker compose -f infra/compose/docker-compose.test.yml up -d --build

      # Wait for goose migrations to complete (condition: service_completed_successfully)
      - name: Wait for migrations
        run: docker compose -f infra/compose/docker-compose.test.yml wait migrate

      # Wait for game + workers health endpoints
      - name: Wait for services healthy
        run: |
          docker compose -f infra/compose/docker-compose.test.yml wait game-test || true
          docker compose -f infra/compose/docker-compose.test.yml wait workers-test || true

      - name: Run E2E tests
        working-directory: frontend
        run: npx playwright test

      - name: Upload Playwright report on failure
        if: failure()
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: playwright-report
          path: frontend/playwright-report/
          retention-days: 7

      - name: Stop test stack
        if: always()
        run: docker compose -f infra/compose/docker-compose.test.yml down -v
Now create root .env.example and update the secrets reference:

# ============================================================
# GSSR — Master environment variable reference
# ============================================================
# This file documents ALL variables used across the project.
# Copy to .env and fill in values for your environment.
#
# Variables are split by destination:
#   [CI]    → GitHub Actions Secrets / Variables (Settings → Secrets and variables)
#   [LOCAL] → Only needed for local development
#   [AUTO]  → Computed/derived by CI from other values, not set directly
# ============================================================


# ────────────────────────────────────────────
# INFRASTRUCTURE PASSWORDS  [CI + LOCAL]
# ────────────────────────────────────────────

POSTGRES_PASSWORD=changeme
# Strong password for PostgreSQL. Used by: postgres, game, workers, goose.
# Generate: openssl rand -hex 24

RABBITMQ_PASS=changeme
# RabbitMQ password for the `gssr` user.
# Generate: openssl rand -hex 16

# MinIO root password (min 8 chars).
# Generate: openssl rand -hex 16


# ────────────────────────────────────────────
# APPLICATION SECRETS  [CI + LOCAL]
# ────────────────────────────────────────────

JWT_SECRET=replace-with-64-char-random-string-generate-with-openssl
# Shared between game service (access/refresh tokens) and workers (admin JWT).
# Must be identical on all Zynq nodes and Main PC.
# Generate: openssl rand -hex 32

LIVEKIT_API_KEY=devkey
# LiveKit API key. Any string; must match livekit.yaml keys section.
# Generate: openssl rand -hex 8

LIVEKIT_API_SECRET=devsecret
# LiveKit API secret (min 32 chars recommended for production).
# Generate: openssl rand -hex 24

GRAFANA_PASSWORD=changeme
# Grafana admin UI password.

# ────────────────────────────────────────────

# Your DockerHub username. Images: <USERNAME>/gssr-game, <USERNAME>/gssr-workers.

# DockerHub access token (not your password).
